// 検 429繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ蟇ｾ遲・ 逕ｻ蜒上・驕・ｻｶ隱ｭ縺ｿ霎ｼ縺ｿ (Lazy Loading) 繧ｪ繝悶じ繝ｼ繝舌・

const imageObserver = new IntersectionObserver((entries, observer) => {
    entries.forEach(entry => {
        if (entry.isIntersecting) {
            const card = entry.target;
            const placeName = card.dataset.placeName;
            const imgEl = card.querySelector('img');

            if (placeName && imgEl && imgEl.src.includes('unsplash.com')) {
                fetchPlacePhoto(placeName).then(url => {
                    if (url) {
                        imgEl.src = url;
                        const place = kinkiPlaces.find(p => p.name === placeName);
                        if (place) place.img = url;
                    }
                });
            }
            observer.unobserve(card);
        }
    });
}, {
    rootMargin: '100px 0px',
    threshold: 0.1
});
// ==========================================
// 検 譛ｬ迚ｩ縺ｮ Google Places API 繧貞他縺ｳ蜃ｺ縺咎未謨ｰ
// ==========================================
window.fetchPlacePhoto = async function (placeName) {
    if (!placeName) return "https://placehold.co/600x400?text=No+Image";

    // 縺吶〒縺ｫ逶ｴ謗･URL縺梧欠螳壹＆繧後※縺・ｋ蝣ｴ蜷医・縺昴・縺ｾ縺ｾ霑斐☆
    if (typeof placeName === 'string' && placeName.startsWith("http")) {
        return placeName;
    }

    try {
        // 縺ゅ↑縺溘′讒狗ｯ峨＠縺・server.js 縺ｮ Places API 繧ｨ繝ｳ繝峨・繧､繝ｳ繝医ｒ蜻ｼ縺ｳ蜃ｺ縺・
        const url = new URL("http://localhost:3000/api/travel/places");

        const response = await fetch(url, {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify({ textQuery: placeName })
        });

        if (!response.ok) throw new Error(`Places API Error: ${response.status}`);
        const data = await response.json();

        // 蜀咏悄繝・・繧ｿ縺瑚ｦ九▽縺九▲縺溷ｴ蜷医《erver.js 邨檎罰縺ｧ蜿門ｾ励☆繧偽RL繧堤函謌・
        if (data.places && data.places.length > 0 && data.places[0].photos && data.places[0].photos.length > 0) {
            const photoName = data.places[0].photos[0].name;
            return `http://localhost:3000/api/travel/photo?name=${encodeURIComponent(photoName)}&maxWidthPx=800`;
        }

    } catch (error) {
        console.error(`[API騾壻ｿ｡繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ] ${placeName} 縺ｮ蜀咏悄蜿門ｾ励↓螟ｱ謨・`, error);
    }

    // 繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ譎ゅｄ蜀咏悄縺後↑縺九▲縺溷ｴ蜷医・繝励Ξ繝ｼ繧ｹ繝帙Ν繝繝ｼ
    return `https://placehold.co/800x600/f1f5f9/64748b?text=${encodeURIComponent(placeName)}`;
};

let currentNameMode = 0;

function getDisplayName(name) {
    const modes = ["kanji", "ruby", "hiragana"];
    const mode = modes[currentNameMode];
    const data = nameDisplayModeMap[name];
    if (data) {
        return data[mode] || name;
    }
    return name;
}

function formatItineraryHtml(text) {
    if (!text) return "";
    let html = text.replace(/&/g, "&amp;").replace(/</g, "&lt;").replace(/>/g, "&gt;");
    html = html.replace(/\n/g, "<br>");
    Object.keys(nameDisplayModeMap).forEach(key => {
        const regex = new RegExp(key, "g");
        html = html.replace(regex, `<span class="place-name" data-original-name="${key}">${getDisplayName(key)}</span>`);
    });
    return html;
}

window.toggleNameDisplayMode = function () {
    currentNameMode = (currentNameMode + 1) % 3;
    const btn = document.getElementById("rubi-switch");
    if (btn) {
        const labels = ["貍｢蟄励・縺ｿ", "貍｢蟄暦ｼ九Ν繝・, "縺ｲ繧峨′縺ｪ"];
        btn.textContent = labels[currentNameMode];
    }
    const placeElements = document.querySelectorAll(".place-name");
    placeElements.forEach(el => {
        const origName = el.getAttribute("data-original-name");
        if (origName) {
            el.innerHTML = getDisplayName(origName);
        }
    });
};

window.tryEnteringApp = function () {
    if (!isSplashAnimationFinished || !isAuthStateResolved) return;

    if (auth.currentUser) {
        const splash = document.getElementById("launch-screen");
        if (splash) {
            splash.classList.add("fade-out");
            setTimeout(() => {
                splash.classList.add("hidden");
                const panel = document.getElementById("onboarding-panel");
                if (panel) {
                    panel.classList.remove("slide-in");
                    panel.classList.add("hidden");
                }
            }, 800);
        }
    } else {
        const splash = document.getElementById("launch-screen");
        if (splash) {
            splash.classList.remove("hidden", "fade-out");
        }
        const panel = document.getElementById("onboarding-panel");
        if (panel) {
            panel.classList.remove("hidden");
            // Force reflow
            void panel.offsetWidth;
            panel.classList.add("slide-in");
        }
    }
};

// 繝ｭ繧ｰ繧､繝ｳ迥ｶ諷九・逶｣隕悶→UI譖ｴ譁ｰ
onAuthStateChanged(auth, (user) => {
    isAuthStateResolved = true;
    updateAuthUI(user);
    if (isSplashAnimationFinished) {
        tryEnteringApp();
    }
});

function updateAuthUI(user) {
    const settingsUserStatus = document.getElementById("settingsUserStatus");
    const settingsAuthBtn = document.getElementById("settingsAuthBtn");
    const shareLoggedOut = document.getElementById("shareLoggedOutState");
    const shareLoggedIn = document.getElementById("shareLoggedInState");

    const nameEl = document.getElementById("userName");
    const statusEl = document.getElementById("userStatus");
    const myPageName = document.getElementById("myPageName");
    const myPageStatus = document.getElementById("myPageStatus");

    if (user) {
        if (user.isAnonymous) {
            // 繧ｲ繧ｹ繝医Ο繧ｰ繧､繝ｳ迥ｶ諷・
            userName = "繧ｲ繧ｹ繝医ヨ繝ｩ繝吶Λ繝ｼ";
            if (nameEl) nameEl.textContent = userName;
            if (statusEl) statusEl.textContent = "繧ｲ繧ｹ繝医Δ繝ｼ繝峨〒蛻ｩ逕ｨ荳ｭ";
            if (myPageName) myPageName.textContent = userName;
            if (myPageStatus) myPageStatus.textContent = "繧ｲ繧ｹ繝医Δ繝ｼ繝峨〒蛻ｩ逕ｨ荳ｭ";

            if (settingsUserStatus) {
                settingsUserStatus.innerHTML = `
                    <div class="auth-status-card logged-out">
                        <span class="material-icons status-icon">account_circle</span>
                        <div>
                            <div class="status-title">繧ｲ繧ｹ繝医ヨ繝ｩ繝吶Λ繝ｼ</div>
                            <div class="status-desc">繝ｭ繧ｰ繧､繝ｳ縺吶ｋ縺ｨ莠亥ｮ壹ｒ繧ｯ繝ｩ繧ｦ繝牙酔譛溘〒縺阪∪縺・/div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                `;
            }
            if (settingsAuthBtn) {
                settingsAuthBtn.innerHTML = `
                    <button class="btn-primary" style="background-color: var(--accent-anmari); width: 100%;" onclick="logoutUser()">
                        <span class="material-icons" style="font-size: 1.1rem; vertical-align: middle; margin-right: 6px;">logout</span>
                        繝ｭ繧ｰ繧｢繧ｦ繝・(繧ｲ繧ｹ繝育ｵゆｺ・
                    </button>
                `;
            }

            // 繧ｲ繧ｹ繝医・蜈ｱ譛画ｩ溯・繧剃ｽｿ縺医↑縺・
            if (shareLoggedOut) shareLoggedOut.classList.remove("hidden");
            if (shareLoggedIn) shareLoggedIn.classList.add("hidden");
        } else {
            // 譛ｬ繝ｭ繧ｰ繧､繝ｳ迥ｶ諷・
            userName = user.displayName || user.email.split('@')[0];
            if (nameEl) nameEl.textContent = userName;
            if (statusEl) statusEl.textContent = "繧｢繧ｫ繧ｦ繝ｳ繝亥酔譛滉ｸｭ (騾｣謳ｺ貂医∩)";
            if (myPageName) myPageName.textContent = userName;
            if (myPageStatus) myPageStatus.textContent = "繧｢繧ｫ繧ｦ繝ｳ繝亥酔譛滉ｸｭ (騾｣謳ｺ貂医∩)";

            if (settingsUserStatus) {
                settingsUserStatus.innerHTML = `
                    <div class="auth-status-card logged-in">
                        <span class="material-icons status-icon">verified_user</span>
                        <div>
                            <div class="status-title">蜷梧悄螳御ｺ・/div>
                            <div class="status-desc">繧｢繧ｫ繧ｦ繝ｳ繝磯｣謳ｺ貂医∩</div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                `;
            }
            if (settingsAuthBtn) {
                settingsAuthBtn.innerHTML = `
                    <button class="btn-primary" style="background-color: var(--accent-anmari); width: 100%;" onclick="logoutUser()">
                        <span class="material-icons" style="font-size: 1.1rem; vertical-align: middle; margin-right: 6px;">logout</span>
                        繝ｭ繧ｰ繧｢繧ｦ繝・
                    </button>
                `;
            }

            // 繝ｭ繧ｰ繧､繝ｳ貂医∩縺ｮ蝣ｴ蜷医・蜈ｱ譛画ｩ溯・繧貞茜逕ｨ蜿ｯ閭ｽ
            if (shareLoggedOut) shareLoggedOut.classList.add("hidden");
            if (shareLoggedIn) shareLoggedIn.classList.remove("hidden");
        }
    } else {
        // 譛ｪ繝ｭ繧ｰ繧､繝ｳ迥ｶ諷・
        userName = localStorage.getItem("kw_username") || "繝医Λ繝吶Λ繝ｼ";
        if (nameEl) nameEl.textContent = userName;
        if (statusEl) statusEl.textContent = "霑醍柄繧ｨ繝ｪ繧｢謗｢邏｢荳ｭ";
        if (myPageName) myPageName.textContent = userName;
        if (myPageStatus) myPageStatus.textContent = "霑醍柄繧ｨ繝ｪ繧｢謗｢邏｢荳ｭ";

        if (settingsUserStatus) {
            settingsUserStatus.innerHTML = `
                <div class="auth-status-card logged-out">
                    <span class="material-icons status-icon">no_accounts</span>
                    <div>
                        <div class="status-title">譛ｪ騾｣謳ｺ</div>
                        <div class="status-desc">繝ｭ繧ｰ繧､繝ｳ縺吶ｋ縺ｨ莠亥ｮ壹ｒ繧ｯ繝ｩ繧ｦ繝牙酔譛溘〒縺阪∪縺・/div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            `;
        }
        if (settingsAuthBtn) {
            settingsAuthBtn.innerHTML = `
                <button class="btn-primary" style="width: 100%;" onclick="openAuthModal()">
                    <span class="material-icons" style="font-size: 1.1rem; vertical-align: middle; margin-right: 6px;">login</span>
                    繧｢繧ｫ繧ｦ繝ｳ繝磯｣謳ｺ / 繝ｭ繧ｰ繧､繝ｳ
                </button>
            `;
        }

        // 譛ｪ繝ｭ繧ｰ繧､繝ｳ縺ｯ蜈ｱ譛画ｩ溯・繧剃ｽｿ縺医↑縺・
        if (shareLoggedOut) shareLoggedOut.classList.remove("hidden");
        if (shareLoggedIn) shareLoggedIn.classList.add("hidden");
    }
}

// ==========================================
// 4. 蛻晄悄蛹門・逅・(繧｢繝励Μ襍ｷ蜍墓凾)
// ==========================================
window.onload = function () {
    initApp();
};

function initApp() {
    // 襍ｷ蜍輔せ繝励Λ繝・す繝･縺ｮ3遘偵ち繧､繝槭・
    setTimeout(() => {
        isSplashAnimationFinished = true;
        if (isAuthStateResolved) {
            tryEnteringApp();
        }
    }, 3000);

    // UI縺ｮ險ｭ螳壼渚譏
    applyTheme(currentTheme);
    applyFontSize(currentFontSize);
    applyAccountSettings();
    document.getElementById("textSizeSlider").value = currentFontSize;
    document.getElementById("settingsUsername").value = userName;
    document.getElementById("settingsHeaderTitle").value = headerTitle;
    document.getElementById("settingsLang").value = currentLanguage;

    const rakutenInput = document.getElementById("settingsRakutenAppId");
    if (rakutenInput) rakutenInput.value = rakutenAppId;

    const geminiInput = document.getElementById("settingsGeminiApiKey");
    if (geminiInput) geminiInput.value = geminiApiKey;

    // 繝・・繝槭・繧ｿ繝ｳ縺ｮ繧｢繧ｯ繝・ぅ繝冶｡ｨ遉ｺ蜷梧悄
    document.querySelectorAll(".theme-btn").forEach(b => b.classList.remove("active"));
    if (currentTheme === "mc-blue") document.getElementById("btnThemeMcBlue")?.classList.add("active");
    if (currentTheme === "mc-emerald") document.getElementById("btnThemeMcEmerald")?.classList.add("active");
    if (currentTheme === "mc-amber") document.getElementById("btnThemeMcAmber")?.classList.add("active");
    if (currentTheme === "mc-dark") document.getElementById("btnThemeMcDark")?.classList.add("active");

    // 縲瑚・蜻ｳ縺ｪ縺励阪Μ繧ｹ繝医・閾ｪ蜍募炎髯､ (15譌･邨碁℃縺励◆繧ゅ・繧偵ヱ繝ｼ繧ｸ)
    purgeOldAnmaris();

    // 讀懃ｴ｢繧ｫ繝ｼ繝峨・繝ｼ繝ｫ縺ｮ貅門ｙ
    applyFilters();

    // 繝帙・繝繧ｫ繧ｦ繝ｳ繝医→繝ｪ繧ｹ繝医・陦ｨ遉ｺ
    updateGridCounts();
    updateCountdown();
    simulateWeather();
    renderSavedSpotsHome();
    renderHomePlans();

    // 繝√Ε繝ｼ繝郁｡ｨ遉ｺ縺ｮ譖ｴ譁ｰ
    updateChart();

    // 蜈ｱ譛峨Μ繧ｹ繝医・譖ｴ譁ｰ
    renderShareView();

    const rubyBtn = document.getElementById("rubi-switch");
    if (rubyBtn) {
        rubyBtn.addEventListener("click", () => {
            toggleNameDisplayMode();
        });
    }
}

function saveToStorage() {
    localStorage.setItem("kw_likes", JSON.stringify(likes));
    localStorage.setItem("kw_anmaris", JSON.stringify(anmaris));
    localStorage.setItem("kw_favorites", JSON.stringify(favorites));
    localStorage.setItem("kw_plans", JSON.stringify(plans));
    localStorage.setItem("kw_username", userName);
    localStorage.setItem("kw_avatar", userAvatar);
    localStorage.setItem("kw_headertitle", headerTitle);
    localStorage.setItem("kw_theme", currentTheme);
    localStorage.setItem("kw_fontsize", currentFontSize);
    localStorage.setItem("kw_lang", currentLanguage);
    localStorage.setItem("kw_rakuten_appid", rakutenAppId);
    localStorage.setItem("kw_gemini_apikey", geminiApiKey);
}
// ==========================================
// 5. 蜈ｱ騾啅I・壹リ繝薙ご繝ｼ繧ｷ繝ｧ繝ｳ繝ｻ繧ｵ繧､繝峨ヰ繝ｼ
// ==========================================
window.toggleSidebar = function () {
    const sidebar = document.getElementById("appSidebar");
    const overlay = document.getElementById("sidebarOverlay");
    sidebar.classList.toggle("open");
    overlay.classList.toggle("open");
};

window.switchView = function (viewId, element) {
    // 蜈ｨ縺ｦ縺ｮView繧帝撼陦ｨ遉ｺ縺ｫ縺吶ｋ
    document.querySelectorAll(".view").forEach(v => v.classList.add("hidden"));

    // 蟇ｾ雎｡縺ｮView繧定｡ｨ遉ｺ縺吶ｋ
    const target = document.getElementById(`view-${viewId}`);
    if (target) target.classList.remove("hidden");

    // 繧ｵ繧､繝峨ヰ繝ｼ縺ｮ繝｡繝九Η繝ｼ鬆・岼縺ｮ繧｢繧ｯ繝・ぅ繝也憾諷区峩譁ｰ
    document.querySelectorAll(".sidebar-item").forEach(item => item.classList.remove("active"));
    if (element) {
        element.classList.add("active");
    } else {
        // 險ｭ螳壹↑縺ｩ縺ｧ螟夜Κ縺九ｉ蜻ｼ縺ｰ繧後◆蝣ｴ蜷医・繧｢繧ｯ繝・ぅ繝夜・岼蜷梧悄
        const items = document.querySelectorAll(".sidebar-item");
        items.forEach(item => {
            const labelText = item.querySelector("span:last-child").textContent;
            if (viewId === "swipe" && labelText.includes("謗｢縺・)) item.classList.add("active");
            if (viewId === "plan" && labelText.includes("莠亥ｮ・)) item.classList.add("active");
            if (viewId === "home" && labelText.includes("繝帙・繝")) item.classList.add("active");
            if (viewId === "mypage" && labelText.includes("繝槭う繝壹・繧ｸ")) item.classList.add("active");
            if (viewId === "settings" && labelText.includes("繝槭う繝壹・繧ｸ")) item.classList.add("active");
        });
    }

    // 蜷・判髱｢迚ｹ譛峨・譖ｴ譁ｰ繝医Μ繧ｬ繝ｼ
    if (viewId === "mypage") {
        updateGridCounts();
        updateChart();
        renderShareView();
    }
    if (viewId === "home") {
        updateGridCounts();
        updateCountdown();
        simulateWeather();
        renderSavedSpotsHome();
        renderHomePlans();
    }
    if (viewId === "plan") {
        renderLikedList();
        renderProactiveSuggestions();

        const proactiveView = document.getElementById("aiProactiveView");
        if (proactiveView) proactiveView.classList.remove("hidden");
        const form = document.getElementById("planForm");
        if (form) form.classList.add("hidden");
        const results = document.getElementById("planResults");
        if (results) results.classList.add("hidden");
        const loading = document.getElementById("planLoading");
        if (loading) loading.classList.add("hidden");
        const err = document.getElementById("planError");
        if (err) err.classList.add("hidden");
    }

    // 繝｢繝舌う繝ｫ逕ｨ繧ｵ繧､繝峨ヰ繝ｼ繧帝哩縺倥ｋ
    const sidebar = document.getElementById("appSidebar");
    const overlay = document.getElementById("sidebarOverlay");
    if (sidebar && sidebar.classList.contains("open")) {
        sidebar.classList.remove("open");
        overlay.classList.remove("open");
    }
};

// Toast騾夂衍陦ｨ遉ｺ
function showToast(message) {
    const container = document.getElementById("toastContainer");
    const toast = document.createElement("div");
    toast.className = "toast";
    toast.innerHTML = `<span class="material-icons" style="font-size: 1.2rem; color: var(--primary-color);">info</span><span>${message}</span>`;
    container.appendChild(toast);

    // 1.2遘貞ｾ後↓繝輔ぉ繝ｼ繝峨い繧ｦ繝医＠縺ｦ蜑企勁
    setTimeout(() => {
        toast.style.transition = "opacity 0.3s ease, transform 0.3s ease";
        toast.style.opacity = "0";
        toast.style.transform = "translateY(-10px)";
        setTimeout(() => toast.remove(), 300);
    }, 1200);
}

// ==========================================
// 6. 讀懃ｴ｢讖溯・ (繧ｹ繝ｯ繧､繝・& 繝励Μ繝輔ぉ繝・メ)
// ==========================================
window.applyFilters = function () {
    const seasonSelect = document.getElementById("filterSeason");
    const catSelect = document.getElementById("filterCategory");

    activeFilters.season = seasonSelect ? seasonSelect.value : "all";
    if (catSelect) {
        activeFilters.category = catSelect.value;
    }

    // 繝輔ぅ繝ｫ繧ｿ譚｡莉ｶ縺ｫ蜷郁・縺吶ｋ繧ｹ繝昴ャ繝医・繝ｼ繝ｫ繧剃ｽ懈・
    currentCardPool = kinkiPlaces.filter(place => {
        const matchSeason = (activeFilters.season === "all" || place.season === activeFilters.season);
        const matchCat = (activeFilters.category === "all" || place.category === activeFilters.category);

        // 縺吶〒縺ｫ縲後＞縺・・縲阪∪縺溘・縲瑚・蜻ｳ縺ｪ縺励阪↓蜈･縺｣縺ｦ縺・ｋ繧ゅ・縺ｯ髯､縺・(繝ｪ繧ｻ繝・ヨ縺輔ｌ縺ｪ縺・剞繧・
        const isAlreadySelected = likes.some(l => l.id === place.id) || anmaris.some(a => a.id === place.id);

        let matchRecommendation = true;
        if (recommendationMode) {
            const highestVal = Math.max(...standStats);
            const highestIndex = standStats.indexOf(highestVal);
            matchRecommendation = matchesGenre(place, highestIndex);
        }

        return matchSeason && matchCat && !isAlreadySelected && matchRecommendation;
    });

    if (recommendationMode) {
        // AI謗ｨ螂ｨ繝｢繝ｼ繝峨・蝣ｴ蜷医√・繝・メ蠎ｦ鬆・↓繧ｽ繝ｼ繝・
        currentCardPool.forEach(place => {
            place.tempCompatibilityScore = calculateCompatibilityScore(place);
        });
        currentCardPool.sort((a, b) => b.tempCompatibilityScore - a.tempCompatibilityScore);
    }

    nextPoolIndex = 0;
    renderStack();
};

window.startPersonalizedSearch = function () {
    calculateStandStats(); // 譛譁ｰ謨ｰ蛟､繧定ｨ育ｮ・
    const highestVal = Math.max(...standStats);
    const highestIndex = standStats.indexOf(highestVal);
    const labels = ["貂ｩ豕峨・逋偵ｄ縺・, "閾ｪ辟ｶ繝ｻ譎ｯ隕ｳ", "豁ｴ蜿ｲ繝ｻ譁・喧", "繧ｰ繝ｫ繝｡", "繧｢繧ｯ繝・ぅ繝薙ユ繧｣", "驛ｽ蟶ゅ・繧ｷ繝ｧ繝・ヴ繝ｳ繧ｰ"];
    const topGenreLabel = labels[highestIndex];

    recommendationMode = true;

    // UI縺ｮ繝舌リ繝ｼ陦ｨ遉ｺ縺ｨ譖ｴ譁ｰ
    const banner = document.getElementById("personalizedRecommendationBanner");
    const genreText = document.getElementById("recommendationGenreName");
    if (banner) banner.classList.remove("hidden");
    if (genreText) genreText.textContent = topGenreLabel;

    showToast(`庁 ${topGenreLabel}迚ｹ蛹悶Ξ繧ｳ繝｡繝ｳ繝峨Δ繝ｼ繝峨ｒ髢句ｧ九＠縺ｾ縺励◆・～);

    // 繧ｹ繝ｯ繧､繝礼判髱｢縺ｫ蛻・ｊ譖ｿ縺医ｋ
    switchView("swipe");
};

window.disableRecommendationMode = function () {
    recommendationMode = false;
    const banner = document.getElementById("personalizedRecommendationBanner");
    if (banner) banner.classList.add("hidden");

    showToast("讓呎ｺ匁､懃ｴ｢繝｢繝ｼ繝峨↓謌ｻ縺励∪縺励◆縲・);
    applyFilters();
};

function matchesGenre(place, genreIndex) {
    if (genreIndex === 0) return place.category === "healing" || place.tags.includes("逋偵ｄ縺・) || place.tags.includes("繝ｪ繝ｩ繝・け繧ｹ");
    if (genreIndex === 1) return place.category === "nature" || place.tags.includes("閾ｪ辟ｶ");
    if (genreIndex === 2) return place.category === "history" || place.tags.includes("豁ｴ蜿ｲ");
    if (genreIndex === 3) return place.category === "food" || place.tags.includes("繧ｰ繝ｫ繝｡");
    if (genreIndex === 4) return place.tags.includes("繧｢繧ｯ繝・ぅ繝・);
    if (genreIndex === 5) return place.tags.includes("驛ｽ蟶・) || place.tags.includes("隕ｳ蜈・);
    return true;
}

function renderStack() {
    const stack = document.getElementById("card-stack");
    const container = document.getElementById("swipeActionsContainer");
    stack.innerHTML = "";

    if (currentCardPool.length === 0) {
        if (container) container.classList.add("hidden");
        stack.innerHTML = `
            <div class="empty-stack-view">
                <span class="material-icons empty-icon">sentiment_dissatisfied</span>
                <h3>隧ｲ蠖薙☆繧玖ｦｳ蜈峨せ繝昴ャ繝医′縺ゅｊ縺ｾ縺帙ｓ</h3>
                <p>繝輔ぅ繝ｫ繧ｿ繝ｼ譚｡莉ｶ繧堤ｷｩ繧√ｋ縺九、I繧剃ｽｿ縺｣縺ｦ譁ｰ縺励￥隕ｳ蜈牙慍繧堤函謌舌＠縺ｦ縺ｿ縺ｾ縺励ｇ縺・ｼ・/p>
                <div class="empty-stack-view-actions">
                    <button class="btn-primary" onclick="generatePlacesWithAI()">笨ｨ AI縺ｧ隕ｳ蜈峨せ繝昴ャ繝医ｒ蠅励ｄ縺・/button>
                    <button class="btn-primary" style="background-color: var(--text-muted); opacity: 0.8;" onclick="resetSwipeHistory()">螻･豁ｴ繧偵Μ繧ｻ繝・ヨ縺励※繧・ｊ逶ｴ縺・/button>
                </div>
            </div>
        `;
        return;
    }

    if (container) container.classList.remove("hidden");

    // 譛蛻昴・繧ｫ繝ｼ繝峨→縲√ヰ繝・け繧ｰ繝ｩ繧ｦ繝ｳ繝峨〒縺ｮ繝励Μ繝輔ぉ繝・メ繧ｫ繝ｼ繝・譛螟ｧ3譫・繧奪OM縺ｫ霑ｽ蜉
    // 驥阪↑繧企・・縺溘ａ縲∝ｾ後ｍ縺ｮ繧ｫ繝ｼ繝峨ｒ蜈医↓謖ｿ蜈･縺吶ｋ
    const cardsToLoad = Math.min(3, currentCardPool.length);
    for (let i = cardsToLoad - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
        const place = currentCardPool[i];
        const card = createCardElement(place, i === 0);
        stack.appendChild(card);
    }
}

// 繧ｫ繝ｼ繝峨・莠句燕隱ｭ縺ｿ霎ｼ縺ｿ (繝励Μ繝輔ぉ繝・メ逕ｻ蜒・
function prefetchNextImages() {
    // 迴ｾ蝨ｨ陦ｨ遉ｺ荳ｭ縺ｮ繧ｫ繝ｼ繝峨・蠕後ｍ縺ｫ謗ｧ縺医※縺・ｋ繧ｫ繝ｼ繝峨・逕ｻ蜒上ｒ繝悶Λ繧ｦ繧ｶ縺ｫ繧ｭ繝｣繝・す繝･縺輔○繧・
    if (currentCardPool.length > 1) {
        const prefetchCount = Math.min(3, currentCardPool.length);
        for (let i = 1; i < prefetchCount; i++) {
            const imgUrl = currentCardPool[i].img;
            const img = new Image();
            img.src = imgUrl;
        }
    }
}

function calculateCompatibilityScore(place) {
    let score = 0;

    // 1. 蜷瑚｡瑚・
    if (place.companion) {
        let maxCompPref = 0;
        place.companion.forEach(c => {
            if (detailedPrefs.companion[c] > maxCompPref) {
                maxCompPref = detailedPrefs.companion[c];
            }
        });
        score += maxCompPref;
    }

    // 2. 莠育ｮ・
    if (place.budget && detailedPrefs.budget[place.budget]) {
        score += detailedPrefs.budget[place.budget];
    }

    // 3. 遘ｻ蜍墓焔谿ｵ
    if (place.transport && detailedPrefs.transport[place.transport]) {
        score += detailedPrefs.transport[place.transport];
    }

    // 4. 逶ｮ逧・
    if (place.purpose && detailedPrefs.purpose[place.purpose]) {
        score += detailedPrefs.purpose[place.purpose];
    }

    let avgScore = Math.round(score / 4);
    return Math.max(30, Math.min(99, avgScore));
}

function createCardElement(data, isTopCard) {
    const card = document.createElement("div");
    card.className = "swipe-card";
    // 陦ｨ遉ｺ蜆ｪ蜈磯・ｽ阪・險ｭ螳夲ｼ亥ｾ・ｩ溘き繝ｼ繝峨ｂ蜷後し繧､繧ｺ繝ｻ蜷御ｽ咲ｽｮ縺ｧ繝輔Λ繝・ヨ縺ｫ驥阪・繧具ｼ・
    card.style.zIndex = isTopCard ? 5 : 1;
    if (!isTopCard) {
        card.style.pointerEvents = "none";
    }

    const isStarred = favorites.some(f => f.id === data.id);
    const isRecommended = recommendationMode;
    const matchScore = calculateCompatibilityScore(data);

    card.innerHTML = `
        <div class="card-img-container">
            <img src="${data.img}" class="card-img" alt="${data.name}">
            <span class="card-prefecture-badge">桃 ${data.prefecture}</span>
            <span class="card-season-badge">高 ${data.season}縺翫☆縺吶ａ</span>
            ${isRecommended ? `<span class="card-match-badge"><span class="material-icons" style="font-size: 0.95rem; vertical-align: middle;">bolt</span>AI繝槭ャ繝∝ｺｦ ${matchScore}%</span>` : ''}
            <div class="swipe-stamp stamp-like">縺・＞縺ｭ</div>
            <div class="swipe-stamp stamp-anmari">闊亥袖縺ｪ縺・/div>
        </div>
        <button class="card-star-btn ${isStarred ? 'starred' : ''}" onclick="toggleFavorite(this, event, ${data.id})"><span class="material-icons-outlined star-icon">${isStarred ? 'star' : 'star_border'}</span></button>
        <div class="card-info">
            <h3><span class="place-name" data-original-name="${data.name}">${getDisplayName(data.name)}</span></h3>
            <div class="card-tags-container">
                <span class="tag-pill"><span class="material-icons">people</span>${data.companion ? data.companion.join('繝ｻ') : ''}</span>
                <span class="tag-pill"><span class="material-icons">payments</span>${data.budget || '繧ｹ繧ｿ繝ｳ繝繝ｼ繝・}</span>
                <span class="tag-pill"><span class="material-icons">commute</span>${data.transport || '蜈ｬ蜈ｱ莠､騾壽ｩ滄未'}</span>
                <span class="tag-pill"><span class="material-icons">explore</span>${data.purpose || '隕ｳ蜈・}</span>
            </div>
            <p>${data.description}</p>
        </div>
    `;

    if (isTopCard) {
        initCardDrag(card, data);
        prefetchNextImages();
    }

    card.dataset.placeName = data.name;
    imageObserver.observe(card);

    return card;
}

window.toggleFavorite = function (starBtn, event, id) {
    event.stopPropagation();
    const item = kinkiPlaces.find(p => p.id === id);
    const starIcon = starBtn.querySelector('.star-icon');
    const index = favorites.findIndex(f => f.id === id);

    if (index > -1) {
        favorites.splice(index, 1);
        starBtn.classList.remove("starred");
        if (starIcon) starIcon.textContent = "star_border";
        showToast("縺頑ｰ励↓蜈･繧翫°繧牙炎髯､縺励∪縺励◆縲・);
    } else {
        favorites.push(item);
        starBtn.classList.add("starred");
        if (starIcon) starIcon.textContent = "star";
        showToast("縺頑ｰ励↓蜈･繧翫↓霑ｽ蜉縺励∪縺励◆・≫ｭ・);

        // Ensure favorited item is also in Saved Spots (likes)
        if (!likes.some(l => l.id === id)) {
            likes.push(item);
        }
    }
    saveToStorage();
    updateGridCounts();
};

function initCardDrag(card, data) {
    let startX = 0, startY = 0;
    let currentX = 0, currentY = 0;
    const stampLike = card.querySelector(".stamp-like");
    const stampAnmari = card.querySelector(".stamp-anmari");

    card.addEventListener("pointerdown", e => {
        // 縺頑ｰ励↓蜈･繧翫・繧ｿ繝ｳ繧偵け繝ｪ繝・け縺励◆譎ゅ・繧ｫ繝ｼ繝峨・繝峨Λ繝・げ繧帝幕蟋九＠縺ｪ縺・
        if (e.target.closest('.card-star-btn')) {
            return;
        }
        isDragging = true;
        startX = e.clientX;
        startY = e.clientY;
        card.style.transition = "none";
        card.setPointerCapture(e.pointerId);
    });

    card.addEventListener("pointermove", e => {
        if (!isDragging) return;
        currentX = e.clientX - startX;
        currentY = e.clientY - startY;

        // 蛯ｾ縺阪→蝗櫁ｻ｢
        const rotate = currentX * 0.08;
        card.style.transform = `translate(${currentX}px, ${currentY}px) rotate(${rotate}deg)`;

        // 繧ｹ繝ｯ繧､繝励せ繧ｿ繝ｳ繝励・騾乗・蠎ｦ繧ｳ繝ｳ繝医Ο繝ｼ繝ｫ
        if (currentX > 30) {
            const opacity = Math.min(1, (currentX - 30) / 100);
            if (stampLike) stampLike.style.opacity = opacity;
            if (stampAnmari) stampAnmari.style.opacity = 0;
        } else if (currentX < -30) {
            const opacity = Math.min(1, (-currentX - 30) / 100);
            if (stampAnmari) stampAnmari.style.opacity = opacity;
            if (stampLike) stampLike.style.opacity = 0;
        } else {
            if (stampLike) stampLike.style.opacity = 0;
            if (stampAnmari) stampAnmari.style.opacity = 0;
        }
    });

    card.addEventListener("pointerup", e => {
        if (!isDragging) return;
        isDragging = false;

        // 繧ｹ繝ｯ繧､繝怜愛螳・(130px莉･荳顔ｧｻ蜍・
        if (Math.abs(currentX) > 130) {
            const dir = currentX > 0 ? "like" : "anmari";
            card.style.transition = "transform 0.4s cubic-bezier(0.25, 1, 0.5, 1), opacity 0.4s ease";
            card.style.transform = `translateX(${currentX > 0 ? 1000 : -1000}px) rotate(${currentX > 0 ? 45 : -45}deg)`;
            card.style.opacity = "0";

            handleSwipeAction(dir, data);

            // 谺｡縺ｮ繧ｫ繝ｼ繝峨∈遘ｻ陦・
            setTimeout(() => {
                card.remove();
                currentCardPool.shift();
                renderStack();
            }, 300);
        } else {
            // 蜈・・菴咲ｽｮ縺ｫ謌ｻ縺・(繝舌ロ縺ｮ繧医≧縺ｪ繧ｹ繝励Μ繝ｳ繧ｰ繧､繝ｼ繧ｸ繝ｳ繧ｰ)
            card.style.transition = "transform 0.45s cubic-bezier(0.175, 0.885, 0.32, 1.2)";
            card.style.transform = "translateX(0) rotate(0deg)";
            if (stampLike) stampLike.style.opacity = 0;
            if (stampAnmari) stampAnmari.style.opacity = 0;
        }
    });
}

function handleSwipeAction(type, data) {
    if (type === "like") {
        if (!likes.some(l => l.id === data.id)) {
            likes.push(data);
            showToast(`笶､・上・{data.name}縲阪ｒ縺・＞縺ｭ縺励∪縺励◆・～);
        }
    } else {
        if (!anmaris.some(a => a.id === data.id)) {
            anmaris.push({ ...data, savedAt: Date.now() });
            showToast(`・縲・{data.name}縲阪・闊亥袖縺ｪ縺励↓縺励∪縺励◆`);
        }
    }
    saveToStorage();
    updateGridCounts();
    // 繧ｹ繧ｿ繝ｳ繝峨ヱ繝ｩ繝｡繝ｼ繧ｿ縺ｮ繝ｪ繧｢繝ｫ繧ｿ繧､繝險育ｮ・
    calculateStandStats();
}

window.resetSwipeHistory = function () {
    likes = [];
    anmaris = [];
    favorites = [];
    plans = [];
    saveToStorage();
    showToast("縺吶∋縺ｦ縺ｮ繧ｹ繝ｯ繧､繝怜ｱ･豁ｴ縺ｨ莠亥ｮ壹ｒ繝ｪ繧ｻ繝・ヨ縺励∪縺励◆縲・);
    applyFilters();
    calculateStandStats();
};

window.swipeTopCard = function (direction) {
    if (currentCardPool.length === 0 || isDragging) return;
    const stack = document.getElementById("card-stack");
    const topCard = stack.querySelector(".swipe-card");
    if (!topCard) return;

    const stampLike = topCard.querySelector(".stamp-like");
    const stampAnmari = topCard.querySelector(".stamp-anmari");

    // 繝舌ャ繧ｸ繧定｡ｨ遉ｺ
    if (direction === "like") {
        if (stampLike) stampLike.style.opacity = "1";
    } else {
        if (stampAnmari) stampAnmari.style.opacity = "1";
    }

    isDragging = true; // 騾｣謇薙ｄ繝峨Λ繝・げ驥崎､・・繝悶Ο繝・け

    topCard.style.transition = "transform 0.45s cubic-bezier(0.25, 1, 0.5, 1), opacity 0.45s ease";
    topCard.style.transform = `translateX(${direction === "like" ? 1000 : -1000}px) rotate(${direction === "like" ? 45 : -45}deg)`;
    topCard.style.opacity = "0";

    const data = currentCardPool[0];
    handleSwipeAction(direction === "like" ? "like" : "anmari", data);

    setTimeout(() => {
        topCard.remove();
        currentCardPool.shift();
        isDragging = false;
        renderStack();
    }, 350);
};

// ==========================================
// 7. 莠亥ｮ壽ｩ溯・ (蜈･蜉帙ユ繝ｳ繝励Ξ繝ｼ繝・& AI繝ｻ繝帙ユ繝ｫ謠先｡・
// ==========================================
function renderLikedList() {
    const listContainer = document.getElementById("likedList");
    if (!listContainer) return;
    listContainer.innerHTML = "";

    if (likes.length === 0) {
        listContainer.innerHTML = `<div class="modal-empty">菫晏ｭ倥＠縺溘せ繝昴ャ繝医′縺ｾ縺縺ゅｊ縺ｾ縺帙ｓ縲ゅ梧爾縺吶阪°繧峨せ繝ｯ繧､繝励＠縺ｦ縺上□縺輔＞縲・/div>`;
        return;
    }

    likes.forEach(item => {
        const isSelected = activePlanTarget && activePlanTarget.id === item.id;
        const div = document.createElement("div");
        div.className = `liked-item ${isSelected ? 'selected' : ''}`;
        div.setAttribute("data-id", item.id);
        div.innerHTML = `
            <img src="${item.img}" class="liked-item-thumb">
            <div class="liked-item-info" style="flex:1; min-width:0;">
                <h4><span class="place-name" data-original-name="${item.name}">${getDisplayName(item.name)}</span></h4>
                <p>桃 ${item.prefecture} / 捷・・${item.season}譎よ悄</p>
            </div>
            <button class="sim3d-launch-mini-btn" title="3D繝ｫ繝ｼ繝医す繝溘Η繝ｬ繝ｼ繧ｷ繝ｧ繝ｳ">
                <span class="material-icons" style="font-size:1.1rem;">route</span>
            </button>
        `;
        div.querySelector(".liked-item-info").addEventListener("click", () => selectPlanTarget(item, div));
        div.querySelector(".sim3d-launch-mini-btn").addEventListener("click", (e) => {
            e.stopPropagation();
            open3DRouteSimulation({ destination: item.name, lat: item.lat, lon: item.lon });
        });
        listContainer.appendChild(div);
    });
}

function selectPlanTarget(item, element) {
    activePlanTarget = item;
    document.querySelectorAll(".liked-item").forEach(i => {
        if (i.getAttribute("data-id") == item.id) {
            i.classList.add("selected");
        } else {
            i.classList.remove("selected");
        }
    });

    // 繝励Ξ繝ｼ繧ｹ繝帙Ν繝繝ｼ縺ｨ蜈亥屓繧願・蜍墓署譯医ン繝･繝ｼ繧帝撼陦ｨ遉ｺ縺ｫ縺励√ヵ繧ｩ繝ｼ繝繧定｡ｨ遉ｺ縺吶ｋ
    const placeholder = document.getElementById("planFormPlaceholder");
    if (placeholder) placeholder.classList.add("hidden");
    const proactiveView = document.getElementById("aiProactiveView");
    if (proactiveView) proactiveView.classList.add("hidden");
    const results = document.getElementById("planResults");
    if (results) results.classList.add("hidden");
    const errorCard = document.getElementById("planError");
    if (errorCard) errorCard.classList.add("hidden");
    const loadingView = document.getElementById("planLoading");
    if (loadingView) loadingView.classList.add("hidden");

    const form = document.getElementById("planForm");
    if (form) form.classList.remove("hidden");
    const targetName = document.getElementById("planTargetName");
    if (targetName) targetName.innerHTML = `<span class="material-icons" style="vertical-align: middle; color: var(--primary-color);">location_on</span> <span class="place-name" data-original-name="${item.name}">${getDisplayName(item.name)}</span> 陦後″譌・｡後・繝ｩ繝ｳ險ｭ螳啻;
}

waypoints縺ｯ譛菴・縺､莉･荳翫・繧ｪ繝悶ず繧ｧ繧ｯ繝医ｒ蜷ｫ縺ｿ縲・・蛻励・譛蛻昴・隕∫ｴ・医う繝ｳ繝・ャ繧ｯ繧ｹ0・峨・蠢・★蜃ｺ逋ｺ蝨ｰ・・{startStation || '螟ｧ髦ｪ繝ｻ譴・伐莉倩ｿ・}・峨・豁｣遒ｺ縺ｪ蠎ｧ讓吶↓縺励※縺上□縺輔＞縲よ怙蠕後・隕∫ｴ縺檎岼逧・慍・・{name}・峨・螳滄圀縺ｮ邱ｯ蠎ｦ邨悟ｺｦ縲√◎縺ｮ髢薙↓譌・ｨ倶ｸ翫・荳ｻ隕∫ｵ檎罰蝨ｰ繧貞性繧√※縺上□縺輔＞縲・
`;

    const requestBody = {
        contents: [{
            parts: [{ text: promptText }]
        }]
    };

    try {
        const resData = await safeFetchJson(url, {
            method: "POST",
            headers: {
                "Content-Type": "application/json"
            },
            body: JSON.stringify(requestBody)
        });
        const rawText = resData.candidates[0].content.parts[0].text;
        const jsonMatch = rawText.match(/\{[\s\S]*\}/);
        if (!jsonMatch) {
            throw new Error("JSON not found in Gemini response");
        }
        return JSON.parse(jsonMatch[0]);
    } catch (error) {
        console.error("Gemini API縺ｧ縺ｮ譌・｡後・繝ｩ繝ｳ逕滓・縺ｫ螟ｱ謨励＠縺ｾ縺励◆:", error);
        throw error;
    }
}



window.togglePriorityPill = function (pill) {
    const val = pill.getAttribute("data-val");
    pill.classList.toggle("active");

    if (pill.classList.contains("active")) {
        if (!currentPriority.includes(val)) currentPriority.push(val);
    } else {
        currentPriority = currentPriority.filter(p => p !== val);
    }
};

window.backToPlanForm = function () {
    document.getElementById("planResults").classList.add("hidden");
    document.getElementById("planForm").classList.remove("hidden");
};

// Base URL for API calls. If page is hosted on a different port (like Live Server at 5500),
// route API requests to the proxy server at http://localhost:3000.
function getApiUrl(path) {
    const base = (window.location.port && window.location.port !== "3000")
        ? "http://localhost:3000"
        : window.location.origin;
    return `${base}${path}`;
}

// Safely fetch and parse JSON, checking response.ok first to avoid JSON parsing errors on HTML/text errors.
async function safeFetchJson(url, options = {}) {
    const response = await fetch(url, options);
    if (!response.ok) {
        let errMsg = `HTTP ${response.status}`;
        try {
            const errData = await response.json();
            errMsg = errData.error || errMsg;
        } catch (e) {
            try {
                const textData = await response.text();
                if (textData && textData.length < 200) {
                    errMsg = textData;
                }
            } catch (textErr) { }
        }
        throw new Error(errMsg);
    }
    return await response.json();
}

// 螳滄圀縺ｮ讌ｽ螟ｩ繝医Λ繝吶ΝAPI繧剃ｸｭ邯吶し繝ｼ繝舌・邨檎罰縺ｧ蜻ｼ縺ｳ蜃ｺ縺咎未謨ｰ
async function fetchRakutenHotels(lat, lon) {
    const cacheKey = `rakuten_hotels_${lat}_${lon}`;
    const cached = sessionStorage.getItem(cacheKey);
    if (cached) {
        console.log("[Rakuten API] Returning cached hotel data");
        return JSON.parse(cached);
    }

    const url = new URL(getApiUrl("/api/travel/hotels"));
    url.searchParams.append("latitude", lat);
    url.searchParams.append("longitude", lon);

    try {
        const data = await safeFetchJson(url.toString());

        if (data.hotels && data.hotels.length > 0) {
            const hotelsList = data.hotels.map(h => {
                const basicInfo = h.hotel?.[0]?.hotelBasicInfo;
                if (!basicInfo) return null;
                return {
                    name: basicInfo.hotelName,
                    rating: basicInfo.reviewAverage || "隧穂ｾ｡縺ｪ縺・,
                    price: basicInfo.hotelMinCharge ? `・･${basicInfo.hotelMinCharge.toLocaleString()}縲彖 : "譁咎≡諠・ｱ縺ｪ縺・,
                    desc: basicInfo.hotelSpecial || "繝励Λ繝ｳ隧ｳ邏ｰ縺ｯ繝ｪ繝ｳ繧ｯ蜈医ｒ縺皮｢ｺ隱阪￥縺縺輔＞縲・,
                    url: basicInfo.hotelInformationUrl,
                    img: basicInfo.hotelImageUrl || ""
                };
            }).filter(Boolean);
            sessionStorage.setItem(cacheKey, JSON.stringify(hotelsList));
            return hotelsList;
        }
        return [];
    } catch (error) {
        console.error("讌ｽ螟ｩ繝医Λ繝吶ΝAPI縺ｮ蜿門ｾ励↓螟ｱ謨励＠縺ｾ縺励◆:", error);
        throw error;
    }
}

// Gemini API繧剃ｸｭ邯吶し繝ｼ繝舌・邨檎罰縺ｧ蜻ｼ縺ｳ蜃ｺ縺励、I繧堤畑縺・※譁ｰ縺励＞隕ｳ蜈牙慍繧堤函謌舌☆繧矩未謨ｰ
async function fetchGeminiPlaces(excludeNames) {
    const url = getApiUrl("/api/travel/generate");
    const excludeStr = excludeNames.length > 0 ? `縺溘□縺励∽ｻ･荳九・隕ｳ蜈牙慍縺ｯ縺吶〒縺ｫ逋ｻ骭ｲ貂医∩縺ｾ縺溘・繧ｹ繝ｯ繧､繝玲ｸ医∩縺ｧ縺ゅｋ縺溘ａ縲∫ｵｶ蟇ｾ縺ｫ蜷ｫ繧√↑縺・〒縺上□縺輔＞: ${excludeNames.join(", ")}` : "";

    const promptText = `
霑醍柄蝨ｰ譁ｹ・亥､ｧ髦ｪ蠎懊∽ｺｬ驛ｽ蠎懊∝・蠎ｫ逵後∝･郁憶逵後∵ｻ玖ｳ逵後∝柱豁悟ｱｱ逵鯉ｼ峨↓縺ゅｋ縲√せ繝ｯ繧､繝怜梛譌・｡後い繝励Μ縺ｧ陦ｨ遉ｺ縺吶ｋ鬲・鴨逧・↑隕ｳ蜈峨せ繝昴ャ繝茨ｼ亥錐謇縲∵ｭｴ蜿ｲ逧・ｻｺ騾迚ｩ縲∵ｸｩ豕峨√げ繝ｫ繝｡陦励∬・辟ｶ縺ｪ縺ｩ・峨ｒ譁ｰ縺溘↓縲・莉ｶ縲崎・｡医＠縲∵律譛ｬ隱槭・JSON蠖｢蠑上〒蜃ｺ蜉帙＠縺ｦ縺上□縺輔＞縲・

${excludeStr}

窶ｻ JSON莉･螟悶・隱ｬ譏取枚繧・・繝ｼ繧ｯ繝繧ｦ繝ｳ縺ｮ繝・さ繝ｬ繝ｼ繧ｷ繝ｧ繝ｳ・・`\`\`json 遲会ｼ峨・荳蛻・性繧√★縲∫ｴ皮ｲ九↑JSON譁・ｭ怜・縺ｮ縺ｿ繧定ｿ斐＠縺ｦ縺上□縺輔＞縲・
`;

    const requestBody = {
        contents: [{
            parts: [{ text: promptText }]
        }],
        generationConfig: {
            responseMimeType: "application/json"
        }
    };

    try {
        const resData = await safeFetchJson(url, {
            method: "POST",
            headers: {
                "Content-Type": "application/json"
            },
            body: JSON.stringify(requestBody)
        });

        const jsonText = resData.candidates?.[0]?.content?.parts?.[0]?.text;
        if (!jsonText) {
            throw new Error("No text candidates in Gemini response");
        }
        const jsonMatch = jsonText.match(/\[[\s\S]*\]/);
        if (!jsonMatch) {
            throw new Error("JSON array not found in Gemini response");
        }
        const newPlaces = JSON.parse(jsonMatch[0]);

        const baseId = Date.now();
        return newPlaces.map((place, idx) => {
            return {
                id: baseId + idx,
                name: place.name,
                prefecture: place.prefecture,
                season: place.season,
                category: place.category,
                description: place.description,
                tags: place.tags || ["隕ｳ蜈・],
                companion: place.companion || ["繧ｫ繝・・繝ｫ"],
                budget: place.budget || "繧ｹ繧ｿ繝ｳ繝繝ｼ繝・,
                transport: place.transport || "蜈ｬ蜈ｱ莠､騾壽ｩ滄未",
                purpose: place.purpose || "繝ｪ繝輔Ξ繝・す繝･",
                lat: place.lat,
                lon: place.lon,
                img: `https://loremflickr.com/500/350/japan,sightseeing,${encodeURIComponent(place.name)}`
            };
        });
    } catch (error) {
        console.error("Gemini API縺ｧ縺ｮ隕ｳ蜈牙慍蜿門ｾ励↓螟ｱ謨励＠縺ｾ縺励◆:", error);
        throw error;
    }
}

// AI縺ｧ縺ｮ隕ｳ蜈牙慍霑ｽ蜉繝懊ち繝ｳ縺ｮ繧｢繧ｯ繧ｷ繝ｧ繝ｳ
window.generatePlacesWithAI = async function () {
    const stack = document.getElementById("card-stack");
    const container = document.getElementById("swipeActionsContainer");
    if (container) container.classList.add("hidden");

    stack.innerHTML = `
        <div class="empty-stack-view" style="animation: fadeIn 0.3s ease;">
            <div class="boat-spinner-container">
                <div class="water-circle"></div>
                <span class="material-icons boat-icon">sailing</span>
            </div>
            <h3 style="margin-top: 16px;">AI縺梧眠縺励＞隕ｳ蜈牙慍繧呈爾邏｢荳ｭ...</h3>
            <p style="font-size: 0.85rem; color: var(--text-muted); margin-bottom: 16px;">霑醍柄蝨ｰ譁ｹ縺ｮ鬲・鴨逧・↑繧ｹ繝昴ャ繝医ｒ逕滓・縺励※縺・∪縺・/p>
            <!-- Shinkansen Progress Bar -->
            <div class="progress-container">
                <div class="progress-bar-track">
                    <div class="progress-bar-fill" id="placesProgressBarFill"></div>
                    <div class="progress-train-icon" id="placesProgressTrain">
                        <span class="material-icons">train</span>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="progress-percentage" id="placesProgressPercent">0%</div>
            </div>
        </div>
    `;

    let progressValue = 0;
    const fill = document.getElementById("placesProgressBarFill");
    const train = document.getElementById("placesProgressTrain");
    const percent = document.getElementById("placesProgressPercent");

    let progressInterval = setInterval(() => {
        if (progressValue < 95) {
            progressValue += Math.floor(Math.random() * 4) + 2;
            if (progressValue > 95) progressValue = 95;
            if (fill) fill.style.width = `${progressValue}%`;
            if (train) train.style.left = `${progressValue}%`;
            if (percent) percent.textContent = `${progressValue}%`;
        }
    }, 80);

    try {
        const existingNames = kinkiPlaces.map(p => p.name);
        const newPlaces = await fetchGeminiPlaces(existingNames);

        clearInterval(progressInterval);
        if (fill) fill.style.width = "100%";
        if (train) train.style.left = "100%";
        if (percent) percent.textContent = "100%";
        await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 300));

        if (newPlaces && newPlaces.length > 0) {
            kinkiPlaces.unshift(...newPlaces);
            showToast("笨ｨ AI縺梧眠縺励＞隕ｳ蜈峨せ繝昴ャ繝医ｒ " + newPlaces.length + " 莉ｶ霑ｽ蜉縺励∪縺励◆・・);
            applyFilters();
        } else {
            throw new Error("Empty list returned");
        }
    } catch (err) {
        clearInterval(progressInterval);
        console.error(err);
        let errorMsgToShow = err.message;
        if (err.message.includes("429")) {
            errorMsgToShow = "譛ｬ譌･縺ｮAI逕滓・荳企剞縺ｫ驕斐＠縺ｾ縺励◆縲よ・譌･縺ｾ縺溘♀隧ｦ縺励￥縺縺輔＞縲・;
        }
        showToast("笞・・閾ｪ蜍慕函謌舌↓螟ｱ謨励＠縺ｾ縺励◆: " + errorMsgToShow);
        stack.innerHTML = `
            <div class="empty-stack-view">
                <span class="material-icons empty-icon">error_outline</span>
                <h3>逕滓・繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ縺檎匱逕溘＠縺ｾ縺励◆</h3>
                <p style="color: var(--accent-error); font-weight: 600;">繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ隧ｳ邏ｰ: ${errorMsgToShow}</p>
                <p>譛ｬ譌･縺ｮ蛻ｩ逕ｨ荳企剞縺ｫ驕斐＠縺溘°縲√し繝ｼ繝舌・蛛ｴ縺ｮ險ｭ螳壹↓蝠城｡後′縺ゅｊ縺ｾ縺吶・/p>
                <div class="empty-stack-view-actions">
                    <button class="btn-primary" onclick="generatePlacesWithAI()">売 蜀崎ｩｦ陦後☆繧・/button>
                    <button class="btn-primary" style="background-color: var(--text-muted); opacity: 0.8;" onclick="resetSwipeHistory()">螻･豁ｴ繧偵Μ繧ｻ繝・ヨ縺励※繧・ｊ逶ｴ縺・/button>
                </div>
            </div>
        `;
    }
};

    "蠖ｦ譬ｹ蝓・: "JR譚ｱ豬ｷ驕捺悽邱夲ｼ育牲逅ｶ貉也ｷ夲ｼ峨悟ｽｦ譬ｹ鬧・阪°繧牙ｾ呈ｭｩ邏・5蛻・ょｽｦ譬ｹ鬧・･ｿ蜿｣繧医ｊ縺雁沁繧ｭ繝｣繝・せ繝ｫ繝ｭ繝ｼ繝臥ｵ檎罰縺ｧ繧｢繧ｯ繧ｻ繧ｹ蜿ｯ閭ｽ縲・,
    "繧｢繝峨・繝ｳ繝√Ε繝ｼ繝ｯ繝ｼ繝ｫ繝・: "JR邏蜍｢譛ｬ邱壹檎區豬憺ｧ・阪°繧画・蜈峨ヰ繧ｹ縺ｧ邏・0蛻・√後い繝峨・繝ｳ繝√Ε繝ｼ繝ｯ繝ｼ繝ｫ繝峨堺ｸ玖ｻ翫☆縺舌ょ､ｧ髦ｪ縺九ｉJR迚ｹ諤･縺上ｍ縺励♀逶ｴ騾壹ｂ縺ゅｊ縲・,
    "辭企㍽蜿､驕・: "荳ｭ霎ｺ霍ｯ繧ｳ繝ｼ繧ｹ縺ｮ襍ｷ轤ｹ縺ｸ縺ｯ縲゛R縲檎ｴ莨雁享豬ｦ鬧・阪∪縺溘・縲梧眠螳ｮ鬧・阪°繧芽ｷｯ邱壹ヰ繧ｹ縺ｧ縲梧ｻ晏ｰｻ邇句ｭ舌阪∪縺溘・縲檎・驥朱ぅ譎ｺ螟ｧ遉ｾ縲阪∈繧｢繧ｯ繧ｻ繧ｹ縲・,
    "螟ｧ髦ｪ蝓主・蝨・: "JR螟ｧ髦ｪ迺ｰ迥ｶ邱壹悟､ｧ髦ｪ蝓主・蝨帝ｧ・阪∪縺溘・縲梧｣ｮ繝主ｮｮ鬧・堺ｸ玖ｻ翫☆縺舌ょ､ｧ髦ｪ繝｡繝医Ο荳ｭ螟ｮ邱壹瑚ｰｷ逕ｺ蝗帑ｸ∫岼鬧・阪°繧峨ｂ繧｢繧ｯ繧ｻ繧ｹ蜿ｯ閭ｽ縲・,
    "豕暮嚀蟇ｺ": "JR髢｢隘ｿ譛ｬ邱壹梧ｳ暮嚀蟇ｺ鬧・阪°繧牙･郁憶莠､騾壹ヰ繧ｹ縲梧ｳ暮嚀蟇ｺ髢蜑阪崎｡後″縺ｧ邏・蛻・∫ｵらせ荳玖ｻ翫☆縺舌ゅ∪縺溘・豕暮嚀蟇ｺ鬧・°繧牙ｾ呈ｭｩ邏・0蛻・・,
    "蝓主ｴ取ｸｩ豕・: "JR螻ｱ髯ｰ譛ｬ邱壹悟沁蟠取ｸｩ豕蛾ｧ・堺ｸ玖ｻ翫・ｧ・燕縺後☆縺先ｸｩ豕芽｡励・荳ｭ蠢・慍縺ｧ縺呻ｼ亥推螟匁ｹｯ縺ｸ縺ｯ蠕呈ｭｩ蝨丞・・峨・,
    "螟ｩ鮴榊ｯｺ": "莠ｬ遖城崕驩・ｵ仙ｱｱ譛ｬ邱夲ｼ亥ｵ宣崕・峨悟ｵ仙ｱｱ鬧・堺ｸ玖ｻ翫☆縺舌・R蠏ｯ蟲ｨ驥守ｷ壹悟ｵｯ蟲ｨ蠏仙ｱｱ鬧・阪°繧牙ｾ呈ｭｩ邏・3蛻・る亂諤･蠏仙ｱｱ邱壹悟ｵ仙ｱｱ鬧・阪°繧牙ｾ呈ｭｩ邏・5蛻・・,
    "逅ｵ逅ｶ貉悶ヰ繝ｬ繧､": "JR貉冶･ｿ邱壹悟ｿ苓ｳ鬧・阪°繧画ｱ溯凶莠､騾壹ヰ繧ｹ縺ｧ邏・0蛻・√後・繧乗ｹ悶ヰ繝ｬ繧､蜑阪堺ｸ玖ｻ翫√Ο繝ｼ繝励え繧ｧ繧､縺ｧ螻ｱ鬆ゅユ繝ｩ繧ｹ縺ｸ・井ｹ苓ｻ顔ｴ・蛻・ｼ峨・,
    "蜈ｭ逕ｲ螻ｱ繝・Λ繧ｹ": "髦ｪ諤･逾樊虻邱壹悟ｾ｡蠖ｱ鬧・阪°繧臥･樊虻蟶ゅヰ繧ｹ16邉ｻ邨ｱ縺ｧ縲悟・逕ｲ繧ｱ繝ｼ繝悶Ν荳矩ｧ・阪∈縲ょ・逕ｲ繧ｱ繝ｼ繝悶Ν縺ｧ螻ｱ鬆ゅ∈逋ｻ繧翫∝・逕ｲ螻ｱ荳翫ヰ繧ｹ縺ｧ縲悟・逕ｲ繧ｬ繝ｼ繝・Φ繝・Λ繧ｹ縲堺ｸ玖ｻ翫・
};



window.generateTravelPlan = async function (event) {
    event.preventDefault();
    if (!activePlanTarget) return;

    const dateVal = document.getElementById("planDate").value;
    const nightsVal = parseInt(document.getElementById("planNights").value);
    const peopleVal = parseInt(document.getElementById("planPeople").value);
    const budgetVal = parseInt(document.getElementById("planBudget").value);
    const othersVal = document.getElementById("planOthers").value;
    const startStationVal = document.getElementById("planStartStation").value;
    const simulateError = false;

    // 繝輔か繝ｼ繝繧帝國縺励※繝ｭ繝ｼ繝・ぅ繝ｳ繧ｰ陦ｨ遉ｺ
    document.getElementById("planForm").classList.add("hidden");
    const loadingView = document.getElementById("planLoading");
    loadingView.classList.remove("hidden");

    // progress bar reset
    let progressValue = 0;
    const fill = document.getElementById("planProgressBarFill");
    const train = document.getElementById("planProgressTrain");
    const percent = document.getElementById("planProgressPercent");
    if (fill) fill.style.width = "0%";
    if (train) train.style.left = "0%";
    if (percent) percent.textContent = "0%";

    // Ensure loading screen is visible to show off animations
    const startTime = Date.now();

    let progressInterval = setInterval(() => {
        if (progressValue < 95) {
            progressValue += Math.floor(Math.random() * 4) + 2;
            if (progressValue > 95) progressValue = 95;
            if (fill) fill.style.width = `${progressValue}%`;
            if (train) train.style.left = `${progressValue}%`;
            if (percent) percent.textContent = `${progressValue}%`;
        }
    }, 80);

    try {
        // 繝・ヰ繝・げ逕ｨ縺ｮ縲窟PI繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ繧貞・迴ｾ縲阪メ繧ｧ繝・け繝懊ャ繧ｯ繧ｹ縺薫N縺ｮ蝣ｴ蜷・
        if (simulateError) {
            throw new Error("Simulated API Error");
        }

        const targetPref = activePlanTarget.prefecture;
        const selectedNightsText = `${nightsVal}豕・{nightsVal + 1}譌･`;

        let itineraryText = "";
        let waypoints = [];
        try {
            const geminiResult = await fetchGeminiItinerary(activePlanTarget.name, targetPref, dateVal, selectedNightsText, peopleVal, budgetVal, currentPriority, othersVal, startStationVal);
            itineraryText = geminiResult.itineraryText || "";
            waypoints = Array.isArray(geminiResult.waypoints) ? geminiResult.waypoints : [];
            showToast("笨ｨ AI縺後≠縺ｪ縺溘・譌・｡後せ繧ｿ繝ｳ繝峨↓蜷医ｏ縺帙◆迚ｹ陬ｽ繝励Λ繝ｳ繧堤函謌舌＠縺ｾ縺励◆・・);
        } catch (apiErr) {
            console.warn("AI繝励Λ繝ｳ逕滓・縺ｫ螟ｱ謨励＠縺溘◆繧√∵耳螂ｨ繝・Φ繝励Ξ繝ｼ繝医ｒ陦ｨ遉ｺ縺励∪縺・", apiErr);
            itineraryText = generateItineraryText(activePlanTarget.name, targetPref, dateVal, selectedNightsText, peopleVal, budgetVal, currentPriority, othersVal);
            showToast("笞・・AI逕滓・蛻ｶ髯舌・縺溘ａ縲∵耳螂ｨ繝・Φ繝励Ξ繝ｼ繝医〒繝励Λ繝ｳ繧剃ｽ懈・縺励∪縺励◆縲・);
        }

        let startCoords = null;
        try {
            if (startStationVal && startStationVal.trim()) {
                startCoords = await new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
                    if (!window.google || !window.google.maps || !window.google.maps.Geocoder) {
                        reject(new Error("Geocoder not available"));
                        return;
                    }
                    const geocoder = new google.maps.Geocoder();
                    geocoder.geocode({ address: startStationVal }, (results, status) => {
                        if (status === "OK" && results && results[0]) {
                            const loc = results[0].geometry.location;
                            resolve({ lat: loc.lat(), lng: loc.lng() });
                        } else {
                            reject(new Error("Geocoding status: " + status));
                        }
                    });
                });
            }
        } catch (geocodeErr) {
            console.warn("Geocoding failed:", geocodeErr);
        }

        if (startCoords) {
            if (waypoints.length > 0) {
                waypoints[0] = {
                    lat: startCoords.lat,
                    lng: startCoords.lng,
                    name: startStationVal || waypoints[0].name || "蜃ｺ逋ｺ蝨ｰ",
                    description: waypoints[0].description || "蜃ｺ逋ｺ蝨ｰ"
                };
            } else {
                waypoints = [
                    { lat: startCoords.lat, lng: startCoords.lng, name: startStationVal || "蜃ｺ逋ｺ蝨ｰ", description: "蜃ｺ逋ｺ蝨ｰ" },
                    { lat: (startCoords.lat + activePlanTarget.lat) / 2, lng: (startCoords.lng + activePlanTarget.lon) / 2, name: "邨檎罰蝨ｰ", description: "繝ｫ繝ｼ繝井ｸ翫・邨檎罰蝨ｰ" },
                    { lat: activePlanTarget.lat, lng: activePlanTarget.lon, name: activePlanTarget.name, description: "逶ｮ逧・慍" }
                ];
            }
        } else {
            if (waypoints.length > 0) {
                if (typeof waypoints[0].lat !== 'number' || typeof waypoints[0].lng !== 'number') {
                    const fallbackLat = 34.7024;
                    const fallbackLng = 135.4959;
                    waypoints[0] = {
                        lat: fallbackLat,
                        lng: fallbackLng,
                        name: startStationVal || "蜃ｺ逋ｺ蝨ｰ (譴・伐)",
                        description: "蜃ｺ逋ｺ蝨ｰ (繝輔か繝ｼ繝ｫ繝舌ャ繧ｯ)"
                    };
                }
            } else {
                const fallbackLat = 34.7024;
                const fallbackLng = 135.4959;
                waypoints = [
                    { lat: fallbackLat, lng: fallbackLng, name: startStationVal || "蜃ｺ逋ｺ蝨ｰ (譴・伐)", description: "蜃ｺ逋ｺ蝨ｰ (繝輔か繝ｼ繝ｫ繝舌ャ繧ｯ)" },
                    { lat: (fallbackLat + activePlanTarget.lat) / 2, lng: (fallbackLng + activePlanTarget.lon) / 2, name: "邨檎罰蝨ｰ", description: "繝ｫ繝ｼ繝井ｸ翫・邨檎罰蝨ｰ" },
                    { lat: activePlanTarget.lat, lng: activePlanTarget.lon, name: activePlanTarget.name, description: "逶ｮ逧・慍" }
                ];
            }
        }

        // =================================================================
        // 縲舌％縺薙°繧画･ｽ螟ｩ繝医Λ繝吶ΝAPI騾｣謳ｺ縺ｮ蛻・ｲ仙・逅・・
        // =================================================================
        let hotels = [];
        let isHotelFallback = false;
        try {
            // 驕ｸ謚槭＆繧後◆隕ｳ蜈牙慍(activePlanTarget)縺ｮ邱ｯ蠎ｦ(lat)繝ｻ邨悟ｺｦ(lon)繧剃ｸｭ邯吶し繝ｼ繝舌・縺ｫ貂｡縺励※繝帙ユ繝ｫ繧呈､懃ｴ｢縺励∪縺・
            hotels = await fetchRakutenHotels(activePlanTarget.lat, activePlanTarget.lon);
            showToast("笨ｨ 讌ｽ螟ｩ繝医Λ繝吶ΝAPI縺九ｉ蜻ｨ霎ｺ縺ｮ繝帙ユ繝ｫ諠・ｱ繧貞叙蠕励＠縺ｾ縺励◆・・);
        } catch (err) {
            // API蜻ｼ縺ｳ蜃ｺ縺励〒繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ縺瑚ｵｷ縺阪◆蝣ｴ蜷医・縲∝ｾ捺擂縺ｮ繝｢繝・け繝・・繧ｿ縺ｫ繝輔か繝ｼ繝ｫ繝舌ャ繧ｯ・郁・蜍募・繧頑崛縺茨ｼ・
            console.warn("繝帙ユ繝ｫ諠・ｱ縺ｮ蜿門ｾ励↓螟ｱ謨励＠縺溘◆繧√√Δ繝・け繝・・繧ｿ縺ｫ繝輔か繝ｼ繝ｫ繝舌ャ繧ｯ縺励∪縺吶・, err);
            hotels = mockHotels[targetPref] || [];
            isHotelFallback = true;
            if (err.message && err.message.includes("429")) {
                showToast("笞・・譛ｬ譌･縺ｮ繝帙ユ繝ｫ讀懃ｴ｢蛻ｶ髯舌↓驕斐＠縺溘◆繧√√Δ繝・け繝帙ユ繝ｫ繧定｡ｨ遉ｺ縺励∪縺吶・);
            } else {
                showToast("笞・・API謗･邯壹お繝ｩ繝ｼ縺ｮ縺溘ａ縲√Δ繝・け繝帙ユ繝ｫ繧定｡ｨ遉ｺ縺励∪縺吶・);
            }
        }
        // =================================================================

        // 蜿門ｾ励＠縺溘・繝・Ν諠・ｱ繧辿TML縺ｫ謠冗判縺吶ｋ蜃ｦ逅・
        const hotelList = document.getElementById("hotelList");
        hotelList.innerHTML = "";

        if (isHotelFallback) {
            const notice = document.createElement("div");
            notice.className = "fallback-notice-banner";
            notice.innerHTML = `
                <span class="material-icons-outlined" style="font-size: 1.1rem; vertical-align: middle; margin-right: 6px; color: var(--accent-anmari);">cloud_off</span>
                <span style="font-size: 0.8rem; font-weight: 700; color: var(--accent-anmari);">
                    API蛻ｶ髯舌∪縺溘・謗･邯壹お繝ｩ繝ｼ縺ｮ縺溘ａ縲∵耳螂ｨ繝帙ユ繝ｫ・医が繝輔Λ繧､繝ｳ陦ｨ遉ｺ・峨ｒ譯亥・縺励※縺・∪縺吶・
                </span>
            `;
            hotelList.appendChild(notice);
        }

        if (hotels.length === 0) {
            const emptyDiv = document.createElement("div");
            emptyDiv.className = "modal-empty";
            emptyDiv.textContent = "蜻ｨ霎ｺ縺ｫ繝帙ユ繝ｫ縺瑚ｦ九▽縺九ｊ縺ｾ縺帙ｓ縺ｧ縺励◆縲・;
            hotelList.appendChild(emptyDiv);
        } else {
            hotels.forEach(h => {
                const card = document.createElement("div");
                card.className = "hotel-card";
                card.innerHTML = `
                    <img src="${h.img || activePlanTarget.img}" class="hotel-img" alt="${h.name}">
                    <div class="hotel-info">
                        <div>
                            <h4>${h.name}</h4>
                            <div class="hotel-rating">箝・${h.rating} / 讌ｽ螟ｩ繝医Λ繝吶Ν繝ｦ繝ｼ繧ｶ繝ｼ隧穂ｾ｡</div>
                            <p style="font-size: 0.8rem; color: var(--text-muted); margin-bottom: 6px;">${h.desc}</p>
                        </div>
                        <div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center;">
                            <span class="hotel-price">${h.price}</span>
                            <!-- 讌ｽ螟ｩ繝医Λ繝吶Ν縺ｮ螳ｿ隧ｳ邏ｰ繝壹・繧ｸ・・.url・峨∈繝ｪ繝ｳ繧ｯ縺励∪縺・-->
                            <a href="${h.url || 'https://travel.rakuten.co.jp/'}" target="_blank" class="btn-primary" style="padding: 6px 12px; font-size: 0.8rem; text-decoration: none;">遨ｺ螳､遒ｺ隱阪・莠育ｴ・/a>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                `;
                hotelList.appendChild(card);
            });
        }

        const planObj = {
            id: Date.now(),
            destination: activePlanTarget.name,
            prefecture: targetPref,
            date: dateVal,
            nights: nightsVal,
            people: peopleVal,
            budget: budgetVal,
            lat: activePlanTarget.lat,
            lon: activePlanTarget.lon,
            itineraryText: itineraryText,
            waypoints: waypoints
        };
        plans.push(planObj);
        saveToStorage();

        document.getElementById("aiPlanText").innerHTML = formatItineraryHtml(itineraryText);

        // 繧｢繧ｯ繧ｻ繧ｹ諠・ｱ陦ｨ遉ｺ
        const transitText = transitAccessRoutes[activePlanTarget.name] || "蜈ｬ蜈ｱ莠､騾壽ｩ滄未縺ｮ諠・ｱ縺瑚ｦ九▽縺九ｊ縺ｾ縺帙ｓ縺ｧ縺励◆縲りｩｳ邏ｰ縺ｪ繝ｫ繝ｼ繝医・繝翫ン繧｢繝励Μ遲峨〒縺皮｢ｺ隱阪￥縺縺輔＞縲・;
        const transitEl = document.getElementById("aiPlanTransitText");
        if (transitEl) transitEl.textContent = transitText;

        const elapsedTime = Date.now() - startTime;
        const minDuration = 1400;
        if (elapsedTime < minDuration) {
            await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, minDuration - elapsedTime));
        }

        clearInterval(progressInterval);
        if (fill) fill.style.width = "100%";
        if (train) train.style.left = "100%";
        if (percent) percent.textContent = "100%";
        await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 250));

        loadingView.classList.add("hidden");
        document.getElementById("planResults").classList.remove("hidden");

        // 繝帙・繝逕ｻ髱｢縺ｮ繧ｫ繧ｦ繝ｳ繝医ム繧ｦ繝ｳ譖ｴ譁ｰ逕ｨ
        updateCountdown();
        updateGridCounts();

        calculateStandStats();

        bind3DSimButton(planObj);

    } catch (error) {
        clearInterval(progressInterval);
        loadingView.classList.add("hidden");
        document.getElementById("planError").classList.remove("hidden");
        showToast("笞・・繝励Λ繝ｳ菴懈・縺ｫ螟ｱ謨励＠縺ｾ縺励◆縲・);
    }
};

function bind3DSimButton(planData) {
    const btn = document.getElementById("launch3DSimBtn");
    if (btn) {
        const newBtn = btn.cloneNode(true);
        btn.parentNode.replaceChild(newBtn, btn);
        newBtn.addEventListener("click", () => {
            const wps = planData.waypoints || [];
            const labels = wps.map(function(wp, i) {
                if (i === 0) return "蜃ｺ逋ｺ蝨ｰ";
                if (i === wps.length - 1) return planData.destination || "逶ｮ逧・慍";
                return "邨檎罰蝨ｰ" + i;
            });
            const enrichedPlan = Object.assign({}, planData, { waypointLabels: labels });
            open3DRouteSimulation(enrichedPlan);
        });
    }
}

// 蜀崎ｩｦ陦・
window.retryPlanGeneration = function () {
    document.getElementById("planError").classList.add("hidden");
    // 繝輔か繝ｼ繝騾∽ｿ｡繧偵ヨ繝ｪ繧ｬ繝ｼ
    const mockEvent = { preventDefault: () => { } };
    generateTravelPlan(mockEvent);
};

function generateItineraryText(name, pref, date, nightsText, people, budget, priorities, others) {
    const startStr = `縲・{name}繧貞ｷ｡繧・${nightsText} 譌・｡後・繝ｩ繝ｳ縲曾n套 譌･遞・ ${date} 縲・| 則 莠ｺ謨ｰ: ${people}蜷肴ｧ・| 腸 莠育ｮ礼岼螳・ ${budget.toLocaleString()}蜀・ｨ句ｺｦ\n検 驥崎ｦ・ ${priorities.join(", ")}\n`;

    let details = `\n--- 亮・・繧ｹ繧ｱ繧ｸ繝･繝ｼ繝ｫ謠先｡・---\n`;
    details += `笆 1譌･逶ｮ:\n`;
    details += `  繝ｻ蜊亥燕: 蜷・慍縺九ｉ蜃ｺ逋ｺ縲゛R${pref}蜀・・荳ｻ隕・ｧ・↓縺ｦ髮・粋縲・n`;
    details += `  繝ｻ譏ｼ鬟・ 蝨ｰ蜈・・蜷咲肇譁咏炊繧貞ｪ閭ｽ・医♀縺吶☆繧・ ${pref}蜷咲黄繝ｩ繝ｳ繝・ｼ峨・n`;
    details += `  繝ｻ蜊亥ｾ・ ${name}繧定ｦｳ蜈峨ら樟蝨ｰ繧ｬ繧､繝峨ｄ謨｣遲悶・繝・・繧堤援謇九↓縺ｮ繧薙・繧頑爾邏｢縺励※縺上□縺輔＞縲・n`;
    details += `  繝ｻ螟墓婿: 荳玖ｨ倥・謗ｨ阮ｦ繝帙ユ繝ｫ縺ｫ繝√ぉ繝・け繧､繝ｳ縲・n`;
    details += `  繝ｻ螟憺俣: ${priorities.includes("繧ｰ繝ｫ繝｡") ? "蝨ｰ蜈・ｱ域欠縺ｮ髫繧悟ｮｶ蜑ｲ辜ｹ縺ｫ縺ｦ繝・ぅ繝翫・縲・ : "螳ｿ縺ｮ迚ｹ陬ｽ貂ｩ豕峨↓豬ｸ縺九▲縺ｦ遘ｻ蜍輔・逍ｲ繧後ｒ逋偵ｄ縺励∪縺吶・}\n`;

    if (nightsText.includes("2豕・) || nightsText.includes("3豕・)) {
        details += `\n笆 2譌･逶ｮ:\n`;
        details += `  繝ｻ蜊亥燕: 繝帙ユ繝ｫ縺ｧ譛晞｣溷ｾ後∝捉霎ｺ縺ｮ閾ｪ辟ｶ貅｢繧後ｋ髫繧後せ繝昴ャ繝医∈繝上う繧ｭ繝ｳ繧ｰ縲・n`;
        details += `  繝ｻ譏ｼ鬟・ 譎ｯ濶ｲ縺ｮ濶ｯ縺・き繝輔ぉ縺ｧ繝ｭ繝ｼ繧ｫ繝ｫ繧ｹ繧､繝ｼ繝・→霆ｽ鬟溘・n`;
        details += `  繝ｻ蜊亥ｾ・ 霑代￥縺ｮ菴馴ｨ灘梛繝ｯ繝ｼ繧ｯ繧ｷ繝ｧ繝・・縲√∪縺溘・豁ｴ蜿ｲ逧・｡嶺ｸｦ縺ｿ繧呈淵遲悶・n`;
        details += `  繝ｻ螟憺俣: 莨晉ｵｱ蟾･闃ｸ縺ｫ蝗ｲ縺ｾ繧後◆迚ｹ蛻･縺ｪ螳ｿ縺ｫ縺ｦ莨壼ｸｭ譁咏炊縺ｫ闊碁ｼ薙・n`;
    }

    details += `\n笆 譛邨よ律:\n`;
    details += `  繝ｻ蜊亥燕: 繝帙ユ繝ｫ繧偵ｆ縺｣縺上ｊ繝√ぉ繝・け繧｢繧ｦ繝医ょ慍蜈・膚蠎苓｡暦ｼ亥ｸょｴ・峨〒縺雁悄逕｣驕ｸ縺ｳ縲・n`;
    details += `  繝ｻ蜊亥ｾ・ 譌・・繝上う繝ｩ繧､繝医→縺励※縲∫ｵｶ譎ｯ繧ｫ繝輔ぉ縺ｧ縺願幻繧偵＠縺ｦ諤昴＞蜃ｺ繧貞・譛峨・n`;
    details += `  繝ｻ螟墓婿: 鬧・∈遘ｻ蜍輔＠縲∝ｸｰ霍ｯ縺ｸ縲ゅ♀逍ｲ繧梧ｧ倥〒縺励◆・―n`;

    if (others.trim()) {
        details += `\n庁 繝ｦ繝ｼ繧ｶ繝ｼ繝ｪ繧ｯ繧ｨ繧ｹ繝亥渚譏:\n縲・{others}縲阪ｒ閠・・縺励∫ｧｻ蜍墓凾髢薙ｒ繧・▲縺溘ｊ縺ｨ遒ｺ菫昴＠縲√＃蟶梧悍縺ｫ豐ｿ縺｣縺溘Ν繝ｼ繝郁ｨｭ螳壹→縺・◆縺励∪縺励◆縲Ａ;
    }

    return startStr + details;
}

// ==========================================
// 8. 繝帙・繝讖溯・ (縲瑚・蜻ｳ縺ｪ縺励阪ョ繝ｼ繧ｿ閾ｪ蜍募炎髯､ & 邂｡逅・
// ==========================================
function purgeOldAnmaris() {
    const now = Date.now();
    const fifteenDaysMs = 15 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
    const initialCount = anmaris.length;

    anmaris = anmaris.filter(item => {
        const savedTime = item.savedAt || now;
        return (now - savedTime) < fifteenDaysMs;
    });

    saveToStorage();
    const deletedCount = initialCount - anmaris.length;
    if (deletedCount > 0) {
        // 繧上★縺九↓驕・ｉ縺帙※繝医・繧ｹ繝医ｒ陦ｨ遉ｺ
        setTimeout(() => {
            showToast(`ｧｹ 15譌･莉･荳顔ｵ碁℃縺励◆縲瑚・蜻ｳ縺ｪ縺励阪ョ繝ｼ繧ｿ繧・${deletedCount} 莉ｶ閾ｪ蜍輔け繝ｪ繝ｼ繝ｳ繧｢繝・・縺励∪縺励◆縲Ａ);
        }, 1000);
    }
}

function updateGridCounts() {
    const savedEl = document.getElementById("savedSpotsCount");
    const anmariEl = document.getElementById("anmariCount");
    const planEl = document.getElementById("homePlansCount");

    if (savedEl) savedEl.textContent = likes.length;
    if (anmariEl) anmariEl.textContent = anmaris.length;
    if (planEl) planEl.textContent = plans.length;
}

function updateCountdown() {
    const el = document.getElementById("heroCountdownDays");
    const dest = document.getElementById("heroCountdownDest");

    const homeEmptyState = document.getElementById("home-empty-state");
    const homeHeroCard = document.getElementById("home-hero-card");

    if (plans.length === 0) {
        if (homeEmptyState) homeEmptyState.classList.remove("hidden");
        if (homeHeroCard) homeHeroCard.classList.add("hidden");

        const homeCtaBtn = document.getElementById("homeCtaBtn");
        if (homeCtaBtn) {
            if (likes.length > 0) {
                homeCtaBtn.textContent = "縺・＞縺ｭ縺励◆繧ｹ繝昴ャ繝医〒繝励Λ繝ｳ繧剃ｽ懊ｋ";
            } else {
                homeCtaBtn.textContent = "AI縺ｫ谺｡縺ｮ譌・｡後ｒ逶ｸ隲・☆繧・;
            }
        }

        renderSavedSpotsHome();
        renderHomePlans();
        return;
    }

    if (homeEmptyState) homeEmptyState.classList.add("hidden");
    if (homeHeroCard) homeHeroCard.classList.remove("hidden");

    // 譛ｪ譚･縺ｮ莠亥ｮ壹ｒ譌･莉倥〒繧ｽ繝ｼ繝医＠縺ｦ逶ｴ霑代・繧ゅ・繧貞叙蠕・
    const sortedPlans = [...plans].filter(p => new Date(p.date) >= new Date().setHours(0, 0, 0, 0))
        .sort((a, b) => new Date(a.date) - new Date(b.date));

    if (sortedPlans.length === 0) {
        if (el) el.textContent = "-- 譌･";
        if (dest) dest.textContent = "谺｡縺ｮ莠亥ｮ壹ｒ菴懈・縺励※縺ｭ";
        if (homeHeroCard) {
            homeHeroCard.style.backgroundImage = "url('https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1493976040374-85c8e12f0c0e?w=800&auto=format&fit=crop')";
            homeHeroCard.style.backgroundSize = "cover";
            homeHeroCard.style.backgroundPosition = "center";
        }
        renderSavedSpotsHome();
        renderHomePlans();
        return;
    }

    const next = sortedPlans[0];
    const diff = Math.ceil((new Date(next.date) - new Date().setHours(0, 0, 0, 0)) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));

    if (el) {
        if (diff === 0) {
            el.textContent = "莉頑律・・;
        } else {
            el.textContent = `${diff} 譌･`;
        }
    }
    if (dest) dest.textContent = `桃 ${next.destination}`;

    const place = kinkiPlaces.find(p => p.name === next.destination);
    if (place && homeHeroCard) {
        homeHeroCard.style.backgroundImage = `url('${place.img}')`;
        homeHeroCard.style.backgroundSize = "cover";
        homeHeroCard.style.backgroundPosition = "center";
    } else if (homeHeroCard) {
        homeHeroCard.style.backgroundImage = "url('https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1493976040374-85c8e12f0c0e?w=800&auto=format&fit=crop')";
        homeHeroCard.style.backgroundSize = "cover";
        homeHeroCard.style.backgroundPosition = "center";
    }

    renderSavedSpotsHome();
    renderHomePlans();
}

// 螟ｩ豌嶺ｺ亥ｱ繧定｡ｨ遉ｺ縺吶ｋ髢｢謨ｰ (繧ｵ繝ｼ繝舌・荳ｭ邯吶〒譛ｬ迚ｩ縺ｮ繝・・繧ｿ繧貞叙蠕励ゅお繝ｩ繝ｼ譎ゅ・閾ｪ蜍輔〒繝｢繝・け縺ｫ繝輔か繝ｼ繝ｫ繝舌ャ繧ｯ)
async function simulateWeather() {
    const weatherIcon = document.getElementById("heroWeatherIcon");
    const weatherTemp = document.getElementById("heroWeatherTemp");
    const weatherDesc = document.getElementById("heroWeatherDesc");
    const weatherLocation = document.getElementById("heroWeatherLoc");

    if (plans.length === 0) {
        if (weatherIcon) weatherIcon.textContent = "研・・;
        if (weatherTemp) weatherTemp.textContent = "--ﾂｰC";
        if (weatherDesc) weatherDesc.textContent = "莠亥ｮ壹ｒ逋ｻ骭ｲ縺吶ｋ縺ｨ陦ｨ遉ｺ縺輔ｌ縺ｾ縺・;
        if (weatherLocation) weatherLocation.textContent = "逶ｮ逧・慍縺ｮ螟ｩ豌・;
        return;
    }

    const sortedPlans = [...plans].filter(p => new Date(p.date) >= new Date().setHours(0, 0, 0, 0))
        .sort((a, b) => new Date(a.date) - new Date(b.date));

    if (sortedPlans.length === 0) return;
    const next = sortedPlans[0];

    const lat = next.lat || 34.6937;
    const lon = next.lon || 135.5023;
    const cacheKey = `weather_${lat}_${lon}`;
    const cached = sessionStorage.getItem(cacheKey);

    if (cached) {
        console.log("[Weather API] Returning cached weather data");
        const cachedData = JSON.parse(cached);
        if (weatherIcon) weatherIcon.textContent = cachedData.emoji;
        if (weatherTemp) weatherTemp.textContent = cachedData.temp;
        if (weatherDesc) weatherDesc.textContent = cachedData.desc;
        if (weatherLocation) weatherLocation.textContent = `桃 ${next.destination} (${next.prefecture})縺ｮ螟ｩ豌輿;
        return;
    }

    try {
        const url = new URL(getApiUrl("/api/travel/weather"));
        url.searchParams.append("latitude", lat);
        url.searchParams.append("longitude", lon);

        const data = await safeFetchJson(url.toString());

        const tempVal = Math.round(data.main.temp) + "ﾂｰC";
        const descVal = data.weather[0].description;
        const emoji = getWeatherIconEmoji(data.weather[0].icon);

        const weatherResult = {
            temp: tempVal,
            desc: descVal,
            emoji: emoji
        };
        sessionStorage.setItem(cacheKey, JSON.stringify(weatherResult));

        if (weatherIcon) weatherIcon.textContent = emoji;
        if (weatherTemp) weatherTemp.textContent = tempVal;
        if (weatherDesc) weatherDesc.textContent = descVal;
        if (weatherLocation) weatherLocation.textContent = `桃 ${next.destination} (${next.prefecture})縺ｮ螟ｩ豌輿;

    } catch (err) {
        console.warn("譛ｬ迚ｩ縺ｮ螟ｩ豌励ョ繝ｼ繧ｿ縺ｮ蜿門ｾ励↓螟ｱ謨励＠縺溘◆繧√√Δ繝・け繝・・繧ｿ縺ｫ蛻・ｊ譖ｿ縺医∪縺・", err);

        // 驛ｽ蠎懃恁縺ｫ蝓ｺ縺･縺上ム繝溘・螟ｩ蛟・(繝輔か繝ｼ繝ｫ繝舌ャ繧ｯ)
        const weatherData = {
            "莠ｬ驛ｽ": { icon: "減", temp: "19ﾂｰC", desc: "遨上ｄ縺九↑譎ｴ繧後・縺｡阮・寐繧・ },
            "螟ｧ髦ｪ": { icon: "笘・・, temp: "24ﾂｰC", desc: "蠢ｫ譎ｴ繝ｻ邨ｶ螂ｽ縺ｮ鬟溘∋豁ｩ縺肴律蜥・ },
            "蜈ｵ蠎ｫ": { icon: "笞・, temp: "22ﾂｰC", desc: "豬ｷ鬚ｨ縺悟ｿ・慍繧医＞譎ｴ繧・ },
            "螂郁憶": { icon: "ｦ・, temp: "18ﾂｰC", desc: "蟆城岑縺ｮ縺｡譎ｴ繧後∫ｷ代′譏縺医ｋ譌･" },
            "貊玖ｳ": { icon: "笵ｵ", temp: "17ﾂｰC", desc: "逅ｵ逅ｶ貉門捉霎ｺ縺ｯ辷ｽ繧・°縺ｪ蠑ｷ鬚ｨ" },
            "蜥梧ｭ悟ｱｱ": { icon: "濠", temp: "25ﾂｰC", desc: "蜊鈴｢ｨ縺梧囑縺九＞螟乗律" }
        };

        const mockInfo = weatherData[next.prefecture] || { icon: "研・・, temp: "20ﾂｰC", desc: "蠢ｫ驕ｩ縺ｪ譌・｡梧律蜥・ };
        if (weatherIcon) weatherIcon.textContent = mockInfo.icon;
        if (weatherTemp) weatherTemp.textContent = mockInfo.temp;
        if (weatherDesc) weatherDesc.textContent = mockInfo.desc;
        if (weatherLocation) weatherLocation.textContent = `桃 ${next.destination} (${next.prefecture})縺ｮ螟ｩ豌輿;
    }
}

// 螟ｩ豌励い繧､繧ｳ繝ｳ繧ｳ繝ｼ繝峨ｒ邨ｵ譁・ｭ励↓繝槭ャ繝斐Φ繧ｰ縺吶ｋ繝倥Ν繝代・髢｢謨ｰ
function getWeatherIconEmoji(iconCode) {
    if (!iconCode) return "研・・;
    const map = {
        "01": "笘・・, // clear sky
        "02": "笵・, // few clouds
        "03": "笘・ｸ・, // scattered clouds
        "04": "笘・ｸ・, // broken clouds
        "09": "県・・, // shower rain
        "10": "絹・・, // rain
        "11": "笵茨ｸ・, // thunderstorm
        "13": "笶・ｸ・, // snow
        "50": "賢・・  // mist
    };
    const prefix = iconCode.substring(0, 2);
    return map[prefix] || "研・・;
}

// ---------------------------
// 繝帙・繝繧ｹ繝ｩ繧､繝繝ｼ・域ｨｪ繧ｹ繝ｩ繧､繝峨・Nike鬚ｨ・・
// ---------------------------
let currentSlide = 0;
let sliderInterval;

window.goToSlide = function (index) {
    const track = document.getElementById("homeSliderTrack");
    const dots = document.querySelectorAll(".dot");
    if (!track) return;

    // 繝医Λ繝・け繧呈ｨｪ譁ｹ蜷代↓遘ｻ蜍・(蜷・せ繝ｩ繧､繝牙ｹ・・50%縺ｪ縺ｮ縺ｧ縲√う繝ｳ繝・ャ繧ｯ繧ｹ蛟阪＠縺ｦ遘ｻ蜍・
    track.style.transform = `translate3d(-${index * 50}%, 0, 0)`;

    dots.forEach((d, i) => d.classList.toggle("active", i === index));
    currentSlide = index;
};

function startSliderAuto() {
    clearInterval(sliderInterval);
    sliderInterval = setInterval(() => {
        goToSlide((currentSlide + 1) % 2);
    }, 5000);
}

function initSliderSwipe() {
    const wrapper = document.querySelector(".home-slider-wrapper");
    if (!wrapper) return;
    let startX = 0;
    wrapper.addEventListener("pointerdown", e => { startX = e.clientX; });
    wrapper.addEventListener("pointerup", e => {
        const diff = e.clientX - startX;
        if (Math.abs(diff) > 50) {
            const next = diff < 0 ? Math.min(currentSlide + 1, 1) : Math.max(currentSlide - 1, 0);
            goToSlide(next);
            clearInterval(sliderInterval);
            startSliderAuto();
        }
    });
}

// ==========================================
// 9. 繝・・繧ｿ讖溯・ (繧ｹ繧ｿ繝ｳ繝峨ヱ繝ｩ繝｡繝ｼ繧ｿ繝ｭ繧ｸ繝・け)
// ==========================================
let standStats = [50, 50, 50, 50, 50, 50]; // 貂ｩ豕峨・逋偵ｄ縺・ 閾ｪ辟ｶ繝ｻ譎ｯ隕ｳ, 豁ｴ蜿ｲ繝ｻ譁・喧, 繧ｰ繝ｫ繝｡, 繧｢繧ｯ繝・ぅ繝薙ユ繧｣, 驛ｽ蟶ゅ・繧ｷ繝ｧ繝・ヴ繝ｳ繧ｰ
let myChart = null;

function calculateStandStats() {
    let healing = 10;
    let nature = 10;
    let history = 10;
    let food = 10;
    let active = 10;
    let urban = 10;

    // 1. 縺・＞縺ｭ(likes)縺九ｉ縺ｮ蜉邂・
    likes.forEach(item => {
        if (item.category === "healing") healing += 25;
        if (item.category === "nature") nature += 25;
        if (item.category === "history") history += 25;
        if (item.category === "food") food += 25;

        if (item.tags.includes("逋偵ｄ縺・) || item.tags.includes("繝ｪ繝ｩ繝・け繧ｹ")) healing += 15;
        if (item.tags.includes("閾ｪ辟ｶ")) nature += 15;
        if (item.tags.includes("豁ｴ蜿ｲ")) history += 15;
        if (item.tags.includes("繧ｰ繝ｫ繝｡")) food += 15;
        if (item.tags.includes("繧｢繧ｯ繝・ぅ繝・)) active += 30;
        if (item.tags.includes("驛ｽ蟶・) || item.tags.includes("隕ｳ蜈・)) urban += 20;
    });

    // 2. 闊亥袖縺ｪ縺・anmaris)縺九ｉ縺ｮ貂帷ｮ・(蝸懷･ｽ縺ｮ髯､螟悶ｒ陦ｨ迴ｾ)
    anmaris.forEach(item => {
        if (item.category === "healing") healing -= 10;
        if (item.category === "nature") nature -= 10;
        if (item.category === "history") history -= 10;
        if (item.category === "food") food -= 10;

        if (item.tags.includes("逋偵ｄ縺・) || item.tags.includes("繝ｪ繝ｩ繝・け繧ｹ")) healing -= 5;
        if (item.tags.includes("閾ｪ辟ｶ")) nature -= 5;
        if (item.tags.includes("豁ｴ蜿ｲ")) history -= 5;
        if (item.tags.includes("繧ｰ繝ｫ繝｡")) food -= 5;
        if (item.tags.includes("繧｢繧ｯ繝・ぅ繝・)) active -= 10;
        if (item.tags.includes("驛ｽ蟶・) || item.tags.includes("隕ｳ蜈・)) urban -= 8;
    });

    // 3. 莠亥ｮ・plans)縺九ｉ縺ｮ蜉邂・
    plans.forEach(plan => {
        const spot = kinkiPlaces.find(p => p.name === plan.destination);
        if (spot) {
            if (spot.category === "healing") healing += 20;
            if (spot.category === "nature") nature += 20;
            if (spot.category === "history") history += 20;
            if (spot.category === "food") food += 20;

            if (spot.tags.includes("繧｢繧ｯ繝・ぅ繝・)) active += 20;
            if (spot.tags.includes("驛ｽ蟶・) || spot.tags.includes("隕ｳ蜈・)) urban += 15;
        } else {
            healing += 5;
            nature += 5;
            history += 5;
            food += 5;
        }
    });

    // 10縺九ｉ100縺ｮ髢薙↓繧ｯ繝ｩ繝ｳ繝・
    standStats = [
        Math.min(100, Math.max(10, healing)),
        Math.min(100, Math.max(10, nature)),
        Math.min(100, Math.max(10, history)),
        Math.min(100, Math.max(10, food)),
        Math.min(100, Math.max(10, active)),
        Math.min(100, Math.max(10, urban))
    ];

    // 譁ｰ螻樊ｧ繧ｿ繧ｰ・亥酔陦瑚・ 莠育ｮ励Ξ繝ｳ繧ｸ, 遘ｻ蜍墓焔谿ｵ, 逶ｮ逧・・繧ｷ繝ｼ繝ｳ・峨・驥阪∩險育ｮ・
    let companions = { "荳莠ｺ譌・: 0, "繧ｫ繝・・繝ｫ": 0, "蜿倶ｺｺ繧ｰ繝ｫ繝ｼ繝・: 0, "蟄宣｣繧・: 0 };
    let budgets = { "菴惹ｺ育ｮ・: 0, "繧ｹ繧ｿ繝ｳ繝繝ｼ繝・: 0, "繝ｩ繧ｰ繧ｸ繝･繧｢繝ｪ繝ｼ": 0 };
    let transports = { "閾ｪ螳ｶ逕ｨ霆・: 0, "蜈ｬ蜈ｱ莠､騾壽ｩ滄未": 0, "蠕呈ｭｩ": 0 };
    let purposes = { "繝ｪ繝輔Ξ繝・す繝･": 0, "繧｢繧ｯ繝・ぅ繝薙ユ繧｣": 0, "繧ｰ繝ｫ繝｡": 0, "豁ｴ蜿ｲ謗｢險ｪ": 0 };

    let totalCompanions = 0;
    let totalBudgets = 0;
    let totalTransports = 0;
    let totalPurposes = 0;

    function addDetailedWeights(spot, factor) {
        if (spot.companion) {
            spot.companion.forEach(c => {
                companions[c] = (companions[c] || 0) + factor;
                totalCompanions += factor;
            });
        }
        if (spot.budget) {
            budgets[spot.budget] = (budgets[spot.budget] || 0) + factor;
            totalBudgets += factor;
        }
        if (spot.transport) {
            transports[spot.transport] = (transports[spot.transport] || 0) + factor;
            totalTransports += factor;
        }
        if (spot.purpose) {
            purposes[spot.purpose] = (purposes[spot.purpose] || 0) + factor;
            totalPurposes += factor;
        }
    }

    likes.forEach(item => {
        let isFav = favorites.some(f => f.id === item.id);
        addDetailedWeights(item, isFav ? 3 : 1);
    });

    // 蜑ｲ蜷茨ｼ茨ｼ・ｼ峨↓螟画鋤
    if (totalCompanions > 0) {
        for (let k in companions) companions[k] = Math.round((companions[k] / totalCompanions) * 100);
    } else {
        companions = { "荳莠ｺ譌・: 25, "繧ｫ繝・・繝ｫ": 25, "蜿倶ｺｺ繧ｰ繝ｫ繝ｼ繝・: 25, "蟄宣｣繧・: 25 };
    }

    if (totalBudgets > 0) {
        for (let k in budgets) budgets[k] = Math.round((budgets[k] / totalBudgets) * 100);
    } else {
        budgets = { "菴惹ｺ育ｮ・: 33, "繧ｹ繧ｿ繝ｳ繝繝ｼ繝・: 34, "繝ｩ繧ｰ繧ｸ繝･繧｢繝ｪ繝ｼ": 33 };
    }

    if (totalTransports > 0) {
        for (let k in transports) transports[k] = Math.round((transports[k] / totalTransports) * 100);
    } else {
        transports = { "閾ｪ螳ｶ逕ｨ霆・: 33, "蜈ｬ蜈ｱ莠､騾壽ｩ滄未": 34, "蠕呈ｭｩ": 33 };
    }

    if (totalPurposes > 0) {
        for (let k in purposes) purposes[k] = Math.round((purposes[k] / totalPurposes) * 100);
    } else {
        purposes = { "繝ｪ繝輔Ξ繝・す繝･": 25, "繧｢繧ｯ繝・ぅ繝薙ユ繧｣": 25, "繧ｰ繝ｫ繝｡": 25, "豁ｴ蜿ｲ謗｢險ｪ": 25 };
    }

    detailedPrefs = { companion: companions, budget: budgets, transport: transports, purpose: purposes };

    saveToStorage();
    updateStandProfile();
}

function updateStandProfile() {
    const labels = ["貂ｩ豕峨・逋偵ｄ縺・, "閾ｪ辟ｶ繝ｻ譎ｯ隕ｳ", "豁ｴ蜿ｲ繝ｻ譁・喧", "繧ｰ繝ｫ繝｡", "繧｢繧ｯ繝・ぅ繝薙ユ繧｣", "驛ｽ蟶ゅ・繧ｷ繝ｧ繝・ヴ繝ｳ繧ｰ"];
    const highestVal = Math.max(...standStats);
    const highestIndex = standStats.indexOf(highestVal);

    let standName = "繝医Λ繝吶Λ繝ｼ繝ｻ繧ｹ繧ｿ繝ｼ";
    let rankText = "C";

    // 遯∝・縺励◆繧ｹ繝・・繧ｿ繧ｹ縺ｫ蝓ｺ縺･縺上せ繧ｿ繝ｳ繝牙錐逕滓・
    if (highestIndex === 0) standName = "貂ｩ豕峨・螳郁ｭｷ逾・(繧ｹ繝代・繧ｬ繝ｼ繝・ぅ繧｢繝ｳ)";
    else if (highestIndex === 1) standName = "螟ｧ閾ｪ辟ｶ縺ｮ髢区挙閠・(繝輔か繝ｬ繧ｹ繝医・繧ｦ繧ｩ繝ｼ繧ｫ繝ｼ)";
    else if (highestIndex === 2) standName = "豁ｴ蜿ｲ縺ｮ謗｢豎り・(繧ｯ繝ｭ繝九け繝ｫ繝ｻ繧｢繝ｼ繧ｫ繧､繝・";
    else if (highestIndex === 3) standName = "鄒朱｣溘・謾ｯ驟崎・(繧ｰ繝ｫ繝｡繝ｻ繝槭せ繧ｿ繝ｼ)";
    else if (highestIndex === 4) standName = "蜀帝匱縺ｮ繧｢繧ｹ繝ｪ繝ｼ繝・(繝ｯ繧､繝ｫ繝峨・繝√Ε繝ｬ繝ｳ繧ｸ繝｣繝ｼ)";
    else if (highestIndex === 5) standName = "驛ｽ蟶ゅ・繝翫ン繧ｲ繝ｼ繧ｿ繝ｼ (繧｢繝ｼ繝舌Φ繝ｻ繧ｨ繧ｯ繧ｹ繝励Ο繝ｼ繝ｩ繝ｼ)";

    // 繝舌Λ繝ｳ繧ｹ縺瑚憶縺・ｴ蜷・
    const sum = standStats.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0);
    const avg = sum / 6;
    let isBalanced = true;
    standStats.forEach(s => {
        if (Math.abs(s - avg) > 15) isBalanced = false;
    });
    if (isBalanced) {
        standName = "隱ｿ蜥後・譌・ｺｺ (繝上・繝｢繝九い繧ｹ繝ｻ繧ｸ繝｣繝ｼ繝九・)";
    }

    // 繝ｩ繝ｳ繧ｯ豎ｺ螳・
    if (avg >= 85) rankText = "A (雜・･ｵ荳翫ヨ繝ｩ繝吶Λ繝ｼ)";
    else if (avg >= 70) rankText = "B (繧｢繧ｯ繝・ぅ繝悶ヨ繝ｩ繝吶Λ繝ｼ)";
    else if (avg >= 55) rankText = "C (讓呎ｺ也噪繝励Λ繝ｳ繝翫・)";
    else if (avg >= 40) rankText = "D (繝槭う繝壹・繧ｹ譌・ｺｺ)";
    else rankText = "E (逋ｺ螻暮比ｸ翫・蜀帝匱閠・";

    const standNameEl = document.getElementById("standName");
    const standRankEl = document.getElementById("standRank");
    if (standNameEl) standNameEl.textContent = standName;
    if (standRankEl) standRankEl.textContent = `險ｺ譁ｭ隧穂ｾ｡: Rank ${rankText}`;
}

function updateChart() {
    const canvas = document.getElementById("standChart");
    if (!canvas) return;

    calculateStandStats(); // 繝代Λ繝｡繝ｼ繧ｿ繧呈怙譁ｰ縺ｫ蜀崎ｨ育ｮ・

    const ctx = canvas.getContext("2d");
    if (myChart) myChart.destroy();

    // 繝・・繝櫁牡縺ｫ繧医ｋ繝√Ε繝ｼ繝育ｷ壹・濶ｲ螟画峩
    let themeColor = "#007cff";
    if (currentTheme === "mc-emerald") themeColor = "#10b981";
    else if (currentTheme === "mc-amber") themeColor = "#f59e0b";
    else if (currentTheme === "mc-dark") themeColor = "#3b82f6";

    myChart = new Chart(ctx, {
        type: "radar",
        data: {
            labels: ["貂ｩ豕峨・逋偵ｄ縺・, "閾ｪ辟ｶ繝ｻ譎ｯ隕ｳ", "豁ｴ蜿ｲ繝ｻ譁・喧", "繧ｰ繝ｫ繝｡", "繧｢繧ｯ繝・ぅ繝薙ユ繧｣", "驛ｽ蟶ゅ・繧ｷ繝ｧ繝・ヴ繝ｳ繧ｰ"],
            datasets: [{
                data: standStats,
                fill: true,
                backgroundColor: `${themeColor}20`,
                borderColor: themeColor,
                pointBackgroundColor: themeColor,
                pointBorderColor: "#fff",
                pointHoverBackgroundColor: "#fff",
                pointHoverBorderColor: themeColor
            }]
        },
        options: {
            scales: {
                r: {
                    min: 0,
                    max: 100,
                    ticks: { display: false, stepSize: 20 },
                    grid: { color: "rgba(255,255,255,0.08)" },
                    angleLines: { color: "rgba(255,255,255,0.08)" },
                    pointLabels: { color: "#94a3b8", font: { family: "sans-serif", size: 12 } }
                }
            },
            plugins: {
                legend: { display: false }
            }
        }
    });

    renderDetailedPrefBars();
}

function renderDetailedPrefBars() {
    const companionContainer = document.getElementById("companionPrefBars");
    const budgetContainer = document.getElementById("budgetPrefBars");
    const transportContainer = document.getElementById("transportPrefBars");
    const purposeContainer = document.getElementById("purposePrefBars");

    if (!companionContainer || !budgetContainer || !transportContainer || !purposeContainer) return;

    function buildBarsHTML(obj) {
        // 蛟､縺ｮ螟ｧ縺阪＞鬆・↓繧ｽ繝ｼ繝・
        const sorted = Object.entries(obj).sort((a, b) => b[1] - a[1]);
        return sorted.map(([key, val]) => `
            <div class="pref-bar-row" style="display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 8px; font-size: 0.75rem; margin-bottom: 6px;">
                <span style="width: 85px; text-align: left; font-weight: 600; color: var(--text-color);">${key}</span>
                <div style="flex: 1; height: 8px; background: rgba(255,255,255,0.06); border-radius: 4px; overflow: hidden; border: 1px solid var(--border-color); position: relative;">
                    <div style="width: ${val}%; height: 100%; background: linear-gradient(90deg, var(--primary-color), #3b82f6); border-radius: 4px; transition: width 0.6s cubic-bezier(0.25, 0.8, 0.25, 1);"></div>
                </div>
                <span style="width: 35px; text-align: right; color: var(--text-muted); font-weight: 600;">${val}%</span>
            </div>
        `).join("");
    }

    companionContainer.innerHTML = buildBarsHTML(detailedPrefs.companion);
    budgetContainer.innerHTML = buildBarsHTML(detailedPrefs.budget);
    transportContainer.innerHTML = buildBarsHTML(detailedPrefs.transport);
    purposeContainer.innerHTML = buildBarsHTML(detailedPrefs.purpose);
}
